    AddButton(Tab0o, {
     Name = "jump & speed",
    Callback = function()
	  local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local TweenService = game:GetService("TweenService")

-- Create GUI
local screenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
screenGui.Name = "SpeedGui"
screenGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
screenGui.Parent = player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")

-- Toggle Button
local toggleBtn = Instance.new("TextButton")
toggleBtn.Name = "ToggleButton"
toggleBtn.Size = UDim2.new(0, 60, 0, 30)
toggleBtn.Position = UDim2.new(0, 10, 0, 10)
toggleBtn.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(60, 60, 60)
toggleBtn.Text = "Menu"
toggleBtn.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
toggleBtn.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
toggleBtn.TextSize = 16
toggleBtn.Parent = screenGui

-- Create Main Frame
local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
frame.Name = "SpeedFrame"
frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 180)
frame.Position = UDim2.new(0.5, -100, 0.5, -90) -- Initial position
frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40)
frame.Active = true
frame.Draggable = true
frame.Visible = true
frame.Parent = screenGui

local tweenInfo = TweenInfo.new(0.4, Enum.EasingStyle.Sine, Enum.EasingDirection.Out)

-- Store original position
local lastPosition = frame.Position

-- Toggle Logic with Tween and remember position
local isVisible = true
toggleBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	if isVisible then
		lastPosition = frame.Position
		local tweenOut = TweenService:Create(frame, tweenInfo, {Position = UDim2.new(lastPosition.X.Scale, lastPosition.X.Offset, 1, 0)})
		tweenOut:Play()
		tweenOut.Completed:Wait()
		frame.Visible = false
	else
		frame.Position = UDim2.new(lastPosition.X.Scale, lastPosition.X.Offset, 1, 0)
		frame.Visible = true
		local tweenIn = TweenService:Create(frame, tweenInfo, {Position = lastPosition})
		tweenIn:Play()
	end
	isVisible = not isVisible
end)

-- GUI Elements (same as before, just shortened comment-wise for clarity)
local madeBy = Instance.new("TextLabel", frame)
madeBy.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0, 16)
madeBy.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, 0)

-- Button logic
continueBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	local speed = tonumber(speedBox.Text)
	local jump = tonumber(jumpBox.Text)
	local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
	local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
	if humanoid then
		if speed and speed >= 0 then humanoid.WalkSpeed = speed end
		if jump and jump >= 0 then humanoid.JumpPower = jump end
	end
end)

resetBtn.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
	local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
	local humanoid = character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
	if humanoid then
		humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
		humanoid.JumpPower = 50
	end
	speedBox.Text = ""
	jumpBox.Text = ""
end)
  end

  AddButton(Tab0o, {
     Name = "báº¥t tá»­",
    Callback = function()
	  local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local Player = Players.LocalPlayer
local Character = Player.Character or Player.CharacterAdded:Wait()

local function makeImmortal()
    if Character then
        -- Báº£o vá»‡ Humanoid
        local humanoid = Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
        if humanoid then
            humanoid.BreakJointsOnDeath = false
            
            -- NgÄƒn cháº·n damage
            humanoid.HealthChanged:Connect(function()
                if humanoid.Health < humanoid.MaxHealth then
                    humanoid.Health = humanoid.MaxHealth
                end
            end)
            
            -- VÃ´ hiá»‡u hÃ³a fall damage
            humanoid.StateChanged:Connect(function(oldState, newState)
                if newState == Enum.HumanoidStateType.FallingDown or 
                   newState == Enum.HumanoidStateType.Dead then
                    humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running)
                end
            end)
            
            print("God Mode activated!")
        end
        
        -- Báº£o vá»‡ khá»i tool damage
        for _, part in pairs(Character:GetChildren()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                part.CanCollide = true
                part.Material = EnumMaterial.ForceField
            end
        end
    end
end

-- KÃ­ch hoáº¡t khi spawn
makeImmortal()

-- KÃ­ch hoáº¡t láº¡i khi respawn
Player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(newChar)
    Character = newChar
    wait(1) -- Chá» character load Ä‘áº§y Ä‘á»§
    makeImmortal()
end)
  end
  })
  local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local Player = Players.LocalPlayer

local noclip = false
local connection

local function noclipLoop()
    local character = Player.Character
    if character and noclip then
        for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                part.CanCollide = false
            end
        end
    end
end

local function toggleNoClip()
    noclip = not noclip
    
    if noclip then
        connection = RunService.Stepped:Connect(noclipLoop)
    else
        if connection then
            connection:Disconnect()
        end
        -- KhÃ´i phá»¥c collision
        local character = Player.Character
        if character then
            for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                    part.CanCollide = true
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Gá»i hÃ m nÃ y Ä‘á»ƒ báº­t/táº¯t NoClip

  AddButton(Tab0o, {
     Name = "No clip",
    Callback = function()
	  toggleNoClip();
  end
  })
  
  
  AddButton(Tab0o, {
     Name = "Inf jump",
    Callback = function()
	  --[[
	WARNING: Heads up! This script has not been verified by ScriptBlox. Use at your own risk!
]]
-- Infinite Auto-Jump Script
-- Author: [Your Name]

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local Player = Players.LocalPlayer
local Character = Player.Character or Player.CharacterAdded:Wait()

local Humanoid = Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")

-- Function to jump continuously
local function autoJump()
    if Humanoid.Jump then
        Humanoid:ChangeState("Jumping")
    end
end

-- Connect the auto-jump function to the Heartbeat event
game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(autoJump)

-- Print a message to indicate the script is running
print("Infinite Auto-Jump Script loaded!")
  end
  })

		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Landed,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Physics,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.PlatformStanding,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Ragdoll,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.RunningNoPhysics,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.StrafingNoPhysics,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Swimming,true)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.RunningNoPhysics)
	else 
		nowe = true



		for i = 1, speeds do
			spawn(function()

				local hb = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat	


				tpwalking = true
				local chr = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
				local hum = chr and chr:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
				while tpwalking and hb:Wait() and chr and hum and hum.Parent do
					if hum.MoveDirection.Magnitude > 0 then
						chr:TranslateBy(hum.MoveDirection)
					end
				end

			end)
		end
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
		local Char = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
		local Hum = Char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid") or Char:FindFirstChildOfClass("AnimationController")

		for i,v in next, Hum:GetPlayingAnimationTracks() do
			v:AdjustSpeed(0)
		end
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Climbing,false)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.FallingDown,false)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Flying,false)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Freefall,false)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp,false)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Jumping,false)

		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.PlatformStanding,false)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Ragdoll,false)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Running,false)
		speaker.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.RunningNoPhysics,false)

		local flying = true
		local deb = true
		local ctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		local lastctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		local maxspeed = 50
		local speed = 0


		local bg = Instance.new("BodyGyro", torso)
		bg.P = 9e4
		bg.maxTorque = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9)
		bg.cframe = torso.CFrame
		local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", torso)
		bv.velocity = Vector3.new(0,0.1,0)
		bv.maxForce = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9)
		if nowe == true then
			plr.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = true
		end
		while nowe == true or game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health == 0 do
			game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()

			if ctrl.l + ctrl.r ~= 0 or ctrl.f + ctrl.b ~= 0 then
				speed = speed+.5+(speed/maxspeed)
				if speed > maxspeed then
					speed = maxspeed
				end
			elseif not (ctrl.l + ctrl.r ~= 0 or ctrl.f + ctrl.b ~= 0) and speed ~= 0 then
				speed = speed-1
				if speed < 0 then
					speed = 0
				end
			end
			if (ctrl.l + ctrl.r) ~= 0 or (ctrl.f + ctrl.b) ~= 0 then
				bv.velocity = ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.lookVector * (ctrl.f+ctrl.b)) + ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.new(ctrl.l+ctrl.r,(ctrl.f+ctrl.b)*.2,0).p) - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p))*speed
				lastctrl = {f = ctrl.f, b = ctrl.b, l = ctrl.l, r = ctrl.r}
			elseif (ctrl.l + ctrl.r) == 0 and (ctrl.f + ctrl.b) == 0 and speed ~= 0 then
				bv.velocity = ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.lookVector * (lastctrl.f+lastctrl.b)) + ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.new(lastctrl.l+lastctrl.r,(lastctrl.f+lastctrl.b)*.2,0).p) - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p))*speed
			else
				bv.velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
			end
			--	game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
			bg.cframe = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.Angles(-math.rad((ctrl.f+ctrl.b)*50*speed/maxspeed),0,0)
		end
		ctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		lastctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		speed = 0
		bg:Destroy()
		bv:Destroy()
		plr.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = false
		tpwalking = false




	else
		local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		local UpperTorso = plr.Character.UpperTorso
		local flying = true
		local deb = true
		local ctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		local lastctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		local maxspeed = 50
		local speed = 0


		local bg = Instance.new("BodyGyro", UpperTorso)
		bg.P = 9e4
		bg.maxTorque = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9)
		bg.cframe = UpperTorso.CFrame
		local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", UpperTorso)
		bv.velocity = Vector3.new(0,0.1,0)
		bv.maxForce = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9)
		if nowe == true then
			plr.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = true
		end
		while nowe == true or game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health == 0 do
			wait()

			if ctrl.l + ctrl.r ~= 0 or ctrl.f + ctrl.b ~= 0 then
				speed = speed+.5+(speed/maxspeed)
				if speed > maxspeed then
					speed = maxspeed
				end
			elseif not (ctrl.l + ctrl.r ~= 0 or ctrl.f + ctrl.b ~= 0) and speed ~= 0 then
				speed = speed-1
				if speed < 0 then
					speed = 0
				end
			end
			if (ctrl.l + ctrl.r) ~= 0 or (ctrl.f + ctrl.b) ~= 0 then
				bv.velocity = ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.lookVector * (ctrl.f+ctrl.b)) + ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.new(ctrl.l+ctrl.r,(ctrl.f+ctrl.b)*.2,0).p) - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p))*speed
				lastctrl = {f = ctrl.f, b = ctrl.b, l = ctrl.l, r = ctrl.r}
			elseif (ctrl.l + ctrl.r) == 0 and (ctrl.f + ctrl.b) == 0 and speed ~= 0 then
				bv.velocity = ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.lookVector * (lastctrl.f+lastctrl.b)) + ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.new(lastctrl.l+lastctrl.r,(lastctrl.f+lastctrl.b)*.2,0).p) - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p))*speed
			else
				bv.velocity = Vector3.new(0,0,0)
			end

			bg.cframe = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.Angles(-math.rad((ctrl.f+ctrl.b)*50*speed/maxspeed),0,0)
		end
		ctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		lastctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		speed = 0
		bg:Destroy()
		bv:Destroy()
		plr.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = false
		tpwalking = false



	end





end)

-- HÃ m Ä‘Ã³ng bÄƒng ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i
local function freezePlayer(playerName)
    local targetPlayer = nil
    
    -- TÃ¬m ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i theo tÃªn
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if string.lower(player.Name) == string.lower(playerName) or 
           string.lower(player.DisplayName) == string.lower(playerName) then
            targetPlayer = player
            break
        end
    end
    
    if targetPlayer then
        local character = targetPlayer.Character
        if character then
            -- Äáº£m báº£o HumanoidRootPart tá»“n táº¡i
            local humanoidRootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            if not humanoidRootPart then
                wait(0.5)
                humanoidRootPart = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            end
            
            if humanoidRootPart then
                -- Táº¡o Anchored Ä‘á»ƒ Ä‘Ã³ng bÄƒng
                humanoidRootPart.Anchored = true
                
                -- ÄÃ³ng bÄƒng táº¥t cáº£ cÃ¡c pháº§n trong character
                for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
                    if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                        part.Anchored = true
                    end
                end
                
                -- ThÃ´ng bÃ¡o thÃ nh cÃ´ng
                TextBox.Text = "ÄÃ£ Ä‘Ã³ng bÄƒng " .. targetPlayer.Name
                task.wait(2)
                TextBox.Text = "Nháº­p tÃªn ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i"
            end
        end
    else
        -- ThÃ´ng bÃ¡o khÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y
        TextBox.Text = "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i!"
        task.wait(2)
        TextBox.Text = "Nháº­p tÃªn ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i"
    end
end

-- Káº¿t ná»‘i sá»± kiá»‡n nÃºt Ä‘Ã³ng bÄƒng
FreezeButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    local playerName = TextBox.Text
    if playerName and playerName ~= "" and playerName ~= "Nháº­p tÃªn ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i" then
        freezePlayer(playerName)
    end
end)

-- Cho phÃ©p nháº¥n Enter Ä‘á»ƒ Ä‘Ã³ng bÄƒng
TextBox.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
    if enterPressed then
        local playerName = TextBox.Text
        if playerName and playerName ~= "" and playerName ~= "Nháº­p tÃªn ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i" then
            freezePlayer(playerName)
        end
    end
end)

-- KÃ©o tháº£ GUI
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local dragging
local dragInput
local dragStart
local startPos

local function update(input)
    local delta = input.Position - dragStart
    Frame.Position = UDim2.new(startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + delta.X, startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + delta.Y)
end

Frame.InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
    if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
        dragging = true
        dragStart = input.Position
        startPos = Frame.Position
        
        input.Changed:Connect(function()
            if input.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
                dragging = false
            end
        end)
    end
end)

Frame.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
    if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then
        dragInput = input
    end
end)

UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
    if input == dragInput and dragging then
        update(input)
    end
end)

  end

  AddButton(Tab0o, {
     Name = "HÃ o quang sigma",
    Callback = function()
	  -- Script táº¡o hÃ o quang Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n cho nhÃ¢n váº­t (Client-side)
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local Lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")

local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local character = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()

-- MÃ u sáº¯c hÃ o quang (Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n)
local AURA_COLORS = {
    Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50),   -- Äá»
    Color3.fromRGB(50, 255, 50),   -- Xanh lÃ¡
    Color3.fromRGB(50, 50, 255),   -- Xanh dÆ°Æ¡ng
    Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 50),  -- VÃ ng
}

local currentColorIndex = 1
local auraPart = nil
local isAuraActive = false

print("âœ¨ Äang táº¡o hÃ o quang Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n...")

-- Táº¡o hÃ o quang Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n (chá»‰ 1 sphere)
local function createSimpleAura()
    -- XÃ³a aura cÅ© náº¿u cÃ³
    if auraPart and auraPart.Parent then
        auraPart:Destroy()
        auraPart = nil
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o part hÃ o quang
    local sphere = Instance.new("Part")
    sphere.Name = "SimpleAura"
    sphere.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball
    sphere.Size = Vector3.new(10, 10, 10)  -- KÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh
    sphere.Transparency = 0.9  -- Gáº§n trong suá»‘t
    sphere.Color = AURA_COLORS[currentColorIndex]
    sphere.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
    sphere.CanCollide = false
    sphere.Anchored = true  -- Cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh vá»‹ trÃ­
    sphere.CastShadow = false
    sphere.Locked = true
    
    -- ThÃªm point light
    local pointLight = Instance.new("PointLight")
    pointLight.Color = AURA_COLORS[currentColorIndex]
    pointLight.Range = 20
    pointLight.Brightness = 2
    pointLight.Shadows = false
    pointLight.Parent = sphere
    
    -- Gáº¯n vÃ o character
    local hrp = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    sphere.Parent = workspace
    
    auraPart = sphere
    return sphere
end

-- Cáº­p nháº­t vá»‹ trÃ­ hÃ o quang (cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh theo nhÃ¢n váº­t)
local function updateAuraPosition()
    if not isAuraActive or not auraPart or not auraPart.Parent then return end
    
    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if hrp then
        -- Cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh vá»‹ trÃ­ ngay táº¡i nhÃ¢n váº­t
        auraPart.Position = hrp.Position
    end
end

-- Báº­t/táº¯t hÃ o quang
local function toggleAura()
    if isAuraActive then
        -- Táº¯t hÃ o quang
        if auraPart and auraPart.Parent then
            auraPart:Destroy()
            auraPart = nil
        end
        isAuraActive = false
        print("âœ¨ ÄÃ£ táº¯t hÃ o quang")
    else
        -- Báº­t hÃ o quang
        isAuraActive = true
        createSimpleAura()
        print("âœ¨ ÄÃ£ báº­t hÃ o quang")
    end
end

-- Äá»•i mÃ u hÃ o quang
local function changeAuraColor()
    currentColorIndex = currentColorIndex + 1
    if currentColorIndex > #AURA_COLORS then
        currentColorIndex = 1
    end
    
    if isAuraActive and auraPart then
        auraPart.Color = AURA_COLORS[currentColorIndex]
        
        -- Cáº­p nháº­t mÃ u cho light
        local light = auraPart:FindFirstChildOfClass("PointLight")
        if light then
            light.Color = AURA_COLORS[currentColorIndex]
        end
        
        print("ðŸŽ¨ ÄÃ£ Ä‘á»•i mÃ u hÃ o quang")
    end
end

-- Thay Ä‘á»•i kÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c hÃ o quang
local function changeAuraSize(increase)
    if isAuraActive and auraPart then
        local currentSize = auraPart.Size.X
        local newSize
        
        if increase then
            newSize = math.min(currentSize + 2, 20)  -- Max 20
        else
            newSize = math.max(currentSize - 2, 6)   -- Min 6
        end
        
        auraPart.Size = Vector3.new(newSize, newSize, newSize)
        print("ðŸ“ KÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c hÃ o quang: " .. newSize)
    end
end

-- Thay Ä‘á»•i Ä‘á»™ trong suá»‘t
local function changeAuraTransparency(increase)
    if isAuraActive and auraPart then
        local currentTransparency = auraPart.Transparency
        local newTransparency
        
        if increase then
            newTransparency = math.min(currentTransparency + 0.1, 0.95)  -- Gáº§n trong suá»‘t
        else
            newTransparency = math.max(currentTransparency - 0.1, 0.3)   -- Äáº­m hÆ¡n
        end
        
        auraPart.Transparency = newTransparency
        print("âšª Äá»™ trong suá»‘t: " .. string.format("%.1f", newTransparency))
    end
end

-- ChÃ­nh
local function startAura()
    print("âœ¨ Khá»Ÿi Ä‘á»™ng hÃ o quang Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n...")
    
    -- Báº­t hÃ o quang
    toggleAura()
    
    -- Báº¯t Ä‘áº§u cáº­p nháº­t vá»‹ trÃ­
    RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(updateAuraPosition)
    
    print("âœ… HÃ o quang Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n Ä‘Ã£ sáºµn sÃ ng!")
end

-- Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng báº­t khi character cÃ³
if character then
    task.wait(1)
    startAura()
else
    LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(newChar)
        character = newChar
        task.wait(1)
        startAura()
    end)
end

-- Äiá»u khiá»ƒn báº±ng phÃ­m
game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
    if gameProcessed then return end
    
    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.H then
        -- H: Báº­t/táº¯t hÃ o quang
        toggleAura()
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.C then
        -- C: Thay Ä‘á»•i mÃ u
        changeAuraColor()
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Up then
        -- MÅ©i tÃªn lÃªn: TÄƒng kÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c
        changeAuraSize(true)
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Down then
        -- MÅ©i tÃªn xuá»‘ng: Giáº£m kÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c
        changeAuraSize(false)
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Right then
        -- MÅ©i tÃªn pháº£i: TÄƒng trong suá»‘t
        changeAuraTransparency(true)
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Left then
        -- MÅ©i tÃªn trÃ¡i: Giáº£m trong suá»‘t
        changeAuraTransparency(false)
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.R then
        -- R: Reset vá» máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh
        if isAuraActive then
            toggleAura()
            task.wait(0.1)
            toggleAura()
        end
    end
end)

print("=== SIMPLE AURA SCRIPT ===")
print("âœ¨ HÃ o quang Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n - khÃ´ng xoay, khÃ´ng di chuyá»ƒn")

  AddButton(Tab0o, {
     Name = "Spawn zombies",
    Callback = function()
	  -- Script spawn zombie Ä‘áº§y Ä‘á»§ bá»™ pháº­n + AI Ä‘uá»•i theo
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

-- Danh sÃ¡ch zombie
local zombies = {}

-- Táº¡o zombie ngay khi exec
local function spawnZombie()
    -- Láº¥y vá»‹ trÃ­ trÆ°á»›c máº·t player
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then 
        warn("KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y character!")
        return 
    end
    
    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then 
        warn("KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y HumanoidRootPart!")
        return 
    end

    torso.TopSurface = Enum.SurfaceType.Smooth

    leftArm.TopSurface = Enum.SurfaceType.Smooth

    rightArm.TopSurface = Enum.SurfaceType.Smooth

    leftLeg.BottomSurface = Enum.SurfaceType.Smooth

    rightLeg.Name = "Right Leg"

    rightLeg.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Forest green")
    rightLeg.TopSurface = Enum.SurfaceType.Smooth
    rightLeg.BottomSurface = Enum.SurfaceType.Smooth
    rightLeg.Parent = zombie
    
    -- Táº¡o Humanoid
    local humanoid = Instance.new("Humanoid")
    humanoid.WalkSpeed = 12
    humanoid.MaxHealth = 150
    humanoid.Health = 150
    humanoid.Parent = zombie
    
    -- Táº¡o cÃ¡c khá»›p ná»‘i (Motor6D)
    local neck = Instance.new("Motor6D")
    neck.Name = "Neck"
    neck.Part0 = torso
    neck.Part1 = head
    neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1, 0)

    neck.Parent = torso

    rightHip.Parent = torso

    rootJoint.Part0 = rootPart
    rootJoint.Part1 = torso
    rootJoint.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
    rootJoint.C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
    rootJoint.Parent = rootPart
    
    -- Äáº·t primary part
    zombie.PrimaryPart = rootPart
    
    -- Cho zombie vÃ o workspace
    zombie.Parent = workspace
    
    -- Táº¡o TouchInterest cho má»—i part Ä‘á»ƒ gÃ¢y sÃ¡t thÆ°Æ¡ng
    local function addDamageTouch(part)
        part.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
            local humanoid = hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
            local player = Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(hit.Parent)
            
            if humanoid and player and player ~= LocalPlayer then
                humanoid:TakeDamage(10)
            end
        end)
    end
    
    -- ThÃªm TouchInterest cho táº¥t cáº£ cÃ¡c part
    for _, part in ipairs(zombie:GetChildren()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") then
            addDamageTouch(part)
        end
    end
    
    -- ThÃªm vÃ o danh sÃ¡ch zombie
    table.insert(zombies, {model = zombie, humanoid = humanoid})
    
    print("âœ… ÄÃ£ spawn zombie thÃ nh cÃ´ng!")
    return zombie, humanoid
end

-- AI Ä‘uá»•i theo player gáº§n nháº¥t
local function startZombieAI(zombie, humanoid)
    coroutine.wrap(function()
        while zombie and zombie.Parent and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 do
            wait(0.5)
            
            local closestPlayer = nil
            local closestDistance = math.huge
            
            -- TÃ¬m player gáº§n nháº¥t
            for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                if player ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local character = player.Character
                    if character then
                        local targetHRP = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if targetHRP then
                            local distance = (targetHRP.Position - zombie.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude
                            if distance < closestDistance then
                                closestDistance = distance
                                closestPlayer = player
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            
            -- Náº¿u tÃ¬m tháº¥y player, Ä‘uá»•i theo
            if closestPlayer and closestPlayer.Character then
                local target = closestPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if target then
                    humanoid:MoveTo(target.Position)
                end
            end
        end
    end)()
end

-- Spawn zombie Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn ngay khi exec
task.wait(0.5) -- Äá»£i má»™t chÃºt Ä‘á»ƒ Ä‘áº£m báº£o character load
local zombie, humanoid = spawnZombie()
if zombie and humanoid then
    startZombieAI(zombie, humanoid)
else
    warn("âŒ KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ spawn zombie!")
end

-- ThÃªm option spawn thÃªm zombie khi nháº¥n F
game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:Connect(function(input)
    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.F then
        local newZombie, newHumanoid = spawnZombie()
        if newZombie and newHumanoid then
            startZombieAI(newZombie, newHumanoid)
        end
    end
end)

-- AI bay theo player CHÃNH XÃC
local function startGhostAI(ghost, humanoid, bodyVelocity, bodyGyro)
    coroutine.wrap(function()
        local target = LocalPlayer.Character
        local lastUpdate = tick()
        
        while ghost and ghost.Parent and humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 do
            local now = tick()
            local deltaTime = now - lastUpdate
            lastUpdate = now
            
            if target and target.Parent then
                local targetHRP = target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                if targetHRP then
                    -- TÃ­nh vector hÆ°á»›ng tá»›i player
                    local direction = (targetHRP.Position - ghost.PrimaryPart.Position)
                    local distance = direction.Magnitude
                    
                    if distance > 3 then
                        -- Chuáº©n hÃ³a vector vÃ  nhÃ¢n vá»›i tá»‘c Ä‘á»™
                        direction = direction.Unit * 25 -- Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ bay
                        
                        -- Ãp dá»¥ng velocity Ä‘á»ƒ bay tá»›i
                        bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(
                            direction.X,
                            2, -- Bay lÆ¡ lá»­ng má»™t chÃºt
                            direction.Z
                        )
                        
                        -- Xoay ma Ä‘á»ƒ nhÃ¬n vá» player
                        bodyGyro.CFrame = CFrame.new(
                            ghost.PrimaryPart.Position,
                            Vector3.new(targetHRP.Position.X, ghost.PrimaryPart.Position.Y, targetHRP.Position.Z)
                        )
                        
                        -- Cáº­p nháº­t humanoid walk direction
                        humanoid:MoveTo(targetHRP.Position)
                        
                    else
                        -- Náº¿u Ä‘Ã£ quÃ¡ gáº§n, bay vÃ²ng quanh
                        bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(
                            math.sin(now * 2) * 5,
                            1,
                            math.cos(now * 2) * 5
                        )
                    end
                    
                    -- Hiá»‡u á»©ng Ã¡nh sÃ¡ng nháº¥p nhÃ¡y
                    local lights = ghost:GetDescendants()
                    for _, light in ipairs(lights) do
                        if light:IsA("PointLight") then
                            light.Brightness = 1.5 + math.sin(now * 5) * 0.5
                        end
                    end
                end
            else
                -- Náº¿u khÃ´ng cÃ³ target, tÃ¬m player gáº§n nháº¥t
                local closestPlayer = nil
                local closestDistance = math.huge
                
                for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
                    if player.Character then
                        local playerHRP = player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                        if playerHRP then
                            local distance = (playerHRP.Position - ghost.PrimaryPart.Position).Magnitude
                            if distance < closestDistance then
                                closestDistance = distance
                                closestPlayer = player
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end
                
                if closestPlayer then
                    target = closestPlayer.Character
                end
            end
            
            task.wait(0.03) -- Cáº­p nháº­t ráº¥t nhanh Ä‘á»ƒ bÃ¡m sÃ¡t
        end
    end)()
end

-- Spawn ma ngay khi exec

    startGhostAI(ghost, humanoid, bodyVelocity, bodyGyro)
end

    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.G then

        if newGhost and newHumanoid then
            startGhostAI(newGhost, newHumanoid, newBodyVelocity, newBodyGyro)
        end
    end
    
    -- XÃ³a táº¥t cáº£ ma khi nháº¥n H
    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.H then
        for _, ghostData in ipairs(ghosts) do
            if ghostData.model and ghostData.model.Parent then
                ghostData.model:Destroy()
            end
        end
        ghosts = {}
        print("ðŸ§¹ ÄÃ£ xÃ³a táº¥t cáº£ ma!")
    end
end)

-- Gáº¯n cÃ¡c bá»™ pháº­n báº±ng Weld
local function weldPart(part0, part1, offset)
    local weld = Instance.new("Weld")
    weld.Part0 = part0
    weld.Part1 = part1
    weld.C0 = offset
    weld.Parent = part1
end

    while true do
        leftEyeLight.Brightness = 2 + math.sin(tick() * 6) * 1
        rightEyeLight.Brightness = 2 + math.sin(tick() * 6 + 0.5) * 1
        task.wait(0.05)
    end
end)()

-- Hiá»‡u á»©ng cho tay (láº¯c lÆ° nháº¹)
coroutine.wrap(function()
    while true do
        local leftArmWeld = leftArm:FindFirstChildOfClass("Weld")
        local rightArmWeld = rightArm:FindFirstChildOfClass("Weld")
        
        if leftArmWeld and rightArmWeld then
            local wave = math.sin(tick() * 2) * 0.3
            leftArmWeld.C0 = CFrame.new(-1.5, wave, 1) * CFrame.Angles(wave * 0.2, 0, 0)
            rightArmWeld.C0 = CFrame.new(1.5, -wave, 1) * CFrame.Angles(-wave * 0.2, 0, 0)
        end
        
        task.wait(0.1)
    end
end)()

-- Hiá»‡u á»©ng cho Ä‘áº§u (láº¯c nháº¹)
coroutine.wrap(function()
    while true do
        local headWeld = head:FindFirstChildOfClass("Weld")
        if headWeld then
            local bob = math.sin(tick() * 1.5) * 0.05
            headWeld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1.5 + bob, 0)
        end
        task.wait(0.1)
    end
end)()

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local Lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")

-- HÃ m Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture lÃªn má»™t BasePart
local function applyTextureToPart(part)
    if not part:IsA("BasePart") then return end
    
    -- XÃ³a cÃ¡c decal cÅ©
    for _, child in ipairs(part:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("Decal") then
            child:Destroy()
        end
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o decal cho 6 máº·t
    local faces = {
        Enum.NormalId.Front,
        Enum.NormalId.Back,
        Enum.NormalId.Left,
        Enum.NormalId.Right,
        Enum.NormalId.Top,
        Enum.NormalId.Bottom
    }
    
    for _, face in ipairs(faces) do
        local decal = Instance.new("Decal")
        decal.Name = "ImageTexture"
        decal.Texture = IMAGE_ID
        decal.Face = face
        decal.Parent = part
    end
    
    -- Äá»•i mÃ u part thÃ nh tráº¯ng Ä‘á»ƒ texture hiá»ƒn thá»‹ rÃµ
    part.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    part.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
    part.Transparency = 0
end

-- HÃ m Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture cho character
local function applyToCharacter(character)
    if not character then return end
    
    for _, part in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") then
            applyTextureToPart(part)
        end
    end
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho accessories
    for _, accessory in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
        if accessory:IsA("Accessory") or accessory:IsA("Hat") then
            local handle = accessory:FindFirstChild("Handle")
            if handle and handle:IsA("BasePart") then
                applyTextureToPart(handle)
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Biáº¿n táº¥t cáº£ parts trong workspace
local function applyToWorkspace()
    print("ðŸ”„ Äang Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture cho workspace...")
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho táº¥t cáº£ BasePart trong workspace
    for _, part in ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") and part.Parent ~= LocalPlayer.Character then
            -- TrÃ¡nh Ã¡p dá»¥ng lÃªn character cá»§a ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i khÃ¡c (sáº½ xá»­ lÃ½ sau)
            if not part:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
                applyTextureToPart(part)
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Biáº¿n táº¥t cáº£ players
local function applyToAllPlayers()
    print("ðŸ‘¥ Äang Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture cho ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i...")
    
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player.Character then
            applyToCharacter(player.Character)
        end
        
        -- Káº¿t ná»‘i sá»± kiá»‡n khi player spawn
        player.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
            task.wait(1) -- Äá»£i character load
            applyToCharacter(character)
        end)
    end
end

-- Ãp dá»¥ng texture cho sky
local function applyToSky()
    print("ðŸŒŒ Äang Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture cho sky...")
    
    -- XÃ³a sky hiá»‡n táº¡i
    for _, obj in ipairs(Lighting:GetChildren()) do
        if obj:IsA("Sky") then
            obj:Destroy()
        end
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o sky má»›i vá»›i texture
    local sky = Instance.new("Sky")
    sky.SkyboxBk = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxDn = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxFt = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxLf = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxRt = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxUp = IMAGE_ID
    sky.Parent = Lighting
end

-- Ãp dá»¥ng texture cho terrain
local function applyToTerrain()
    if Workspace:FindFirstChildOfClass("Terrain") then
        print("â›°ï¸ Äang Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture cho terrain...")
        
        local terrain = Workspace:FindFirstChildOfClass("Terrain")
        
        -- Äá»•i mÃ u terrain
        terrain:Clear()
        
        -- Táº¡o má»™t sá»‘ block Ä‘á»ƒ tháº¥y texture
        local region = Region3.new(
            Vector3.new(-100, 0, -100),
            Vector3.new(100, 10, 100)
        )
        
        local materialColors = {}
        for i = 1, 9 do
            materialColors[i] = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        end
        
        terrain:FillRegion(region, 10, Enum.Material.Grass)
    end
end

-- Ãp dá»¥ng texture cho UI elements (náº¿u cÃ³)
local function applyToUI()
    print("ðŸ“± Äang Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture cho UI...")
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho SurfaceGuis
    for _, gui in ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
        if gui:IsA("SurfaceGui") or gui:IsA("BillboardGui") then
            for _, element in ipairs(gui:GetDescendants()) do
                if element:IsA("ImageLabel") or element:IsA("ImageButton") then
                    element.Image = IMAGE_ID
                end
            end
        end
    end
end

-- ChÃ­nh
local function startTextureTransformation()
    print("ðŸš€ Báº¯t Ä‘áº§u biáº¿n Ä‘á»•i texture...")
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho báº£n thÃ¢n trÆ°á»›c
    if LocalPlayer.Character then
        applyToCharacter(LocalPlayer.Character)
    end
    
    LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(character)
        task.wait(1)
        applyToCharacter(character)
    end)
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho workspace
    applyToWorkspace()
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho táº¥t cáº£ players
    applyToAllPlayers()
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho sky
    applyToSky()
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho terrain
    applyToTerrain()
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho UI
    applyToUI()
    
    -- Theo dÃµi vÃ  Ã¡p dá»¥ng cho objects má»›i
    Workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(descendant)
        task.wait(0.1)
        if descendant:IsA("BasePart") then
            if not descendant:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
                applyTextureToPart(descendant)
            end
        end
    end)
    
    print("âœ… ÄÃ£ Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture " .. IMAGE_ID .. " lÃªn má»i thá»©!")
    print("ðŸŽ¨ Táº¥t cáº£ objects, players, sky Ä‘á»u cÃ³ texture nÃ y")
end

    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.R then
        print("ðŸ”„ LÃ m má»›i texture...")
        startTextureTransformation()
    end
end)

-- HÃ m táº¡o skybox tá»« má»™t texture
local function createSkyFromTexture(textureId)
    -- XÃ³a táº¥t cáº£ sky hiá»‡n cÃ³
    for _, sky in ipairs(Lighting:GetChildren()) do
        if sky:IsA("Sky") then
            sky:Destroy()
        end
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o skybox má»›i
    local newSky = Instance.new("Sky")
    newSky.Name = "CustomTextureSky"
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng texture cho cáº£ 6 máº·t cá»§a skybox
    newSky.SkyboxBk = textureId  -- Máº·t sau
    newSky.SkyboxDn = textureId  -- Máº·t dÆ°á»›i
    newSky.SkyboxFt = textureId  -- Máº·t trÆ°á»›c
    newSky.SkyboxLf = textureId  -- Máº·t trÃ¡i
    newSky.SkyboxRt = textureId  -- Máº·t pháº£i
    newSky.SkyboxUp = textureId  -- Máº·t trÃªn
    
    -- TÃ¹y chá»‰nh thÃªm cÃ¡c thuá»™c tÃ­nh sky
    newSky.SunAngularSize = 0  -- áº¨n máº·t trá»i máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh
    newSky.MoonAngularSize = 0  -- áº¨n máº·t trÄƒng máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh
    
    -- Táº¯t cÃ¡c hiá»‡u á»©ng máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh
    newSky.StarCount = 0  -- KhÃ´ng cÃ³ sao
    newSky.SunTextureId = ""  -- KhÃ´ng cÃ³ texture máº·t trá»i
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng cho lighting
    newSky.Parent = Lighting
    
    return newSky
end

-- HÃ m táº¡o cÃ¡c hiá»‡u á»©ng atmosphere
local function createAtmosphereEffects()
    -- XÃ³a atmosphere cÅ©
    for _, atm in ipairs(Lighting:GetChildren()) do
        if atm:IsA("Atmosphere") then
            atm:Destroy()
        end
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o atmosphere má»›i Ä‘á»ƒ Ä‘iá»u chá»‰nh mÃ u sáº¯c
    local atmosphere = Instance.new("Atmosphere")
    atmosphere.Name = "CustomAtmosphere"
    atmosphere.Density = 0.1  -- Äá»™ Ä‘áº·c khÃ­ quyá»ƒn tháº¥p
    atmosphere.Offset = 0.25
    atmosphere.Color = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 255)  -- MÃ u xanh nháº¡t
    atmosphere.Decay = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 200)
    atmosphere.Glare = 0  -- KhÃ´ng cÃ³ chÃ³i
    atmosphere.Haze = 0   -- KhÃ´ng cÃ³ sÆ°Æ¡ng mÃ¹
    atmosphere.Parent = Lighting
end

-- HÃ m Ä‘iá»u chá»‰nh lighting Ä‘á»ƒ phÃ¹ há»£p vá»›i skybox
local function adjustLighting()
    -- Äiá»u chá»‰nh ambient
    Lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)  -- Ãnh sÃ¡ng xung quanh
    Lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150)
    
    -- Äiá»u chá»‰nh mÃ u sáº¯c
    Lighting.Brightness = 1.5  -- TÄƒng Ä‘á»™ sÃ¡ng
    Lighting.GlobalShadows = true  -- Giá»¯ bÃ³ng
    Lighting.ClockTime = 14  -- Giá»¯a trÆ°a Ä‘á»ƒ cÃ³ Ã¡nh sÃ¡ng tá»‘t nháº¥t
    
    -- Táº¯t bloom vÃ  cÃ¡c hiá»‡u á»©ng post-processing khÃ¡c
    if Lighting:FindFirstChild("BloomEffect") then
        Lighting.BloomEffect.Enabled = false
    end
    if Lighting:FindFirstChild("BlurEffect") then
        Lighting.BlurEffect.Enabled = false
    end
end

-- HÃ m táº¡o hiá»‡u á»©ng mÃ¢y Ä‘á»™ng (náº¿u muá»‘n)
local function createCloudEffects()
    -- XÃ³a clouds cÅ©
    for _, cloud in ipairs(Lighting:GetChildren()) do
        if cloud.Name == "Clouds" then
            cloud:Destroy()
        end
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o clouds layer tá»« cÃ¹ng texture
    local clouds = Instance.new("Clouds")
    clouds.Name = "CustomClouds"
    clouds.Cover = 0.3  -- Äá»™ phá»§ mÃ¢y
    clouds.Density = 0.2  -- Máº­t Ä‘á»™ mÃ¢y
    clouds.Color = Color3.fromRGB(220, 220, 220)  -- MÃ u mÃ¢y tráº¯ng
    clouds.Parent = Lighting
end

-- HÃ m chÃ­nh

    -- 3. Äiá»u chá»‰nh lighting

    -- 4. Táº¡o hiá»‡u á»©ng mÃ¢y (tÃ¹y chá»n)

    -- 5. Táº¡o hiá»‡u á»©ng cho sun vÃ  moon (áº©n Ä‘i)

        Lighting.SunRaysEffect.Enabled = false

end

-- HÃ m táº¡o vÃ  phÃ¡t sound
local function playSound()
    -- Dá»«ng sound cÅ© náº¿u cÃ³
    if sound then
        sound:Stop()
        sound:Destroy()
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o sound má»›i
    sound = Instance.new("Sound")
    sound.SoundId = SOUND_ID
    sound.Name = "CustomMusic"
    sound.Volume = 1.0
    sound.Looped = true  -- Láº·p láº¡i
    sound.Parent = SoundService
    
    -- Khi sound loaded
    sound.Loaded:Connect(function()
        print("âœ… ÄÃ£ load sound: " .. SOUND_ID)
        print("ðŸ“Š ThÃ´ng tin sound:")
        print("   ðŸŽšï¸ Volume: " .. sound.Volume)
        print("   â±ï¸ Length: " .. sound.TimeLength .. " giÃ¢y")
        print("   ðŸ” Loop: " .. tostring(sound.Looped))
    end)
    
    -- PhÃ¡t sound
    sound:Play()
    print("â–¶ï¸ Äang phÃ¡t sound...")
    
    return sound
end

-- HÃ m Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn volume
local function setVolume(volume)
    if sound then
        sound.Volume = math.clamp(volume, 0, 10)
        print("ðŸŽšï¸ Volume Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘áº·t: " .. sound.Volume)
    end
end

-- HÃ m pause/resume
local function togglePause()
    if sound then
        if sound.IsPlaying then
            sound:Pause()
            print("â¸ï¸ ÄÃ£ táº¡m dá»«ng")
        else
            sound:Resume()
            print("â–¶ï¸ Tiáº¿p tá»¥c phÃ¡t")
        end
    end
end

-- HÃ m dá»«ng sound
local function stopSound()
    if sound then
        sound:Stop()
        print("â¹ï¸ ÄÃ£ dá»«ng sound")
    end
end

-- PhÃ¡t sound ngay khi exec
local currentSound = playSound()

-- Äiá»u khiá»ƒn báº±ng phÃ­m
game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
    if gameProcessed then return end
    
    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.P then
        -- P: Play/Pause
        togglePause()
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.S then
        -- S: Stop
        stopSound()
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.R then
        -- R: Restart
        currentSound = playSound()
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Up then
        -- MÅ©i tÃªn lÃªn: TÄƒng volume
        if sound then
            setVolume(sound.Volume + 0.1)
        end
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Down then
        -- MÅ©i tÃªn xuá»‘ng: Giáº£m volume
        if sound then
            setVolume(sound.Volume - 0.1)
        end
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.M then
        -- M: Mute/Unmute
        if sound then
            if sound.Volume > 0 then
                sound.Volume = 0
                print("ðŸ”‡ ÄÃ£ táº¯t tiáº¿ng")
            else
                sound.Volume = 1.0
                print("ðŸ”Š ÄÃ£ báº­t tiáº¿ng")
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng phÃ¡t láº¡i khi sound káº¿t thÃºc (náº¿u khÃ´ng loop)
if currentSound then
    currentSound.Ended:Connect(function()
        print("ðŸ”š Sound Ä‘Ã£ káº¿t thÃºc")
        if not currentSound.Looped then
            task.wait(1)
            currentSound = playSound()
        end
    end)
end

-- Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng dá»«ng khi player cháº¿t (tÃ¹y chá»n)
LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
    task.wait(0.5)
    -- CÃ³ thá»ƒ restart sound khi respawn
    -- currentSound = playSound()
end)

print("=== SOUND PLAYER SCRIPT ===")
print("ðŸŽµ Äang phÃ¡t: " .. SOUND_ID)
print("ðŸŽ® Äiá»u khiá»ƒn:")
print("   ðŸ…¿ï¸ P: Play/Pause")
print("   ðŸ†‚ S: Stop")
print("   ðŸ† R: Restart")
print("   ðŸ”¼ MÅ©i tÃªn lÃªn: TÄƒng volume")
print("   ðŸ”½ MÅ©i tÃªn xuá»‘ng: Giáº£m volume")
print("   ðŸ…¼ M: Mute/Unmute")
print("ðŸ” Sound sáº½ láº·p láº¡i vÃ´ háº¡n")

    while true do
        if sound then
            local percent = math.floor(sound.Volume * 100)
            local bar = "[" .. string.rep("â–ˆ", math.floor(percent/10)) .. string.rep("â–‘", 10-math.floor(percent/10)) .. "]"
            print("\rVolume: " .. bar .. " " .. percent .. "%   ", false)
        end
        task.wait(0.5)
    end
end)()
   end

     Callback = function()
       -- Script biáº¿n to x3 ngay khi execute (KhÃ´ng cáº§n báº¥m phÃ­m)
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local SCALE_MULTIPLIER = 3  -- To x3 luÃ´n
local isScaled = false

print("ðŸ’ª Äang biáº¿n to x3 ngay láº­p tá»©c...")

-- Táº¡o RemoteEvent
local scaleRemote
if ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("AutoScaleRemote") then
    scaleRemote = ReplicatedStorage.AutoScaleRemote
else
    scaleRemote = Instance.new("RemoteEvent")
    scaleRemote.Name = "AutoScaleRemote"
    scaleRemote.Parent = ReplicatedStorage
    print("ðŸ“¡ ÄÃ£ táº¡o AutoScaleRemote")
end

-- Táº¡o Server Script tá»± Ä‘á»™ng
local function createServerScript()
    local serverScriptService = game:GetService("ServerScriptService")
    
    if serverScriptService:FindFirstChild("AutoScaleServer") then
        print("âœ… Server script Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i")
        return
    end
    
    local script = Instance.new("Script")
    script.Name = "AutoScaleServer"
    
    script.Source = [[
        local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
        local Players = game:GetService("Players")
        local scaleRemote = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("AutoScaleRemote")
        
        print("ðŸ’ª Auto Scale Server Ä‘Ã£ khá»Ÿi Ä‘á»™ng")
        
        -- Khi nháº­n yÃªu cáº§u scale
        scaleRemote.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, action, scale)
            if action == "scale" then
                print("ðŸ“ˆ " .. player.Name .. " Ä‘Ã£ biáº¿n to x" .. scale)
                -- Gá»­i cho táº¥t cáº£ clients
                scaleRemote:FireAllClients("scale", player, scale)
            end
        end)
        
        print("âœ… Server sáºµn sÃ ng scale")
    ]]
    
    script.Parent = serverScriptService
    print("âœ… ÄÃ£ táº¡o server script tá»± Ä‘á»™ng")
end

-- HÃ m scale máº¡nh máº½
local function applyBigScale(character, scale)
    if not character then 
        print("âš ï¸ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y character")
        return 
    end
    
    print("ðŸ”§ Äang scale character...")
    
    -- Scale táº¥t cáº£ BaseParts
    for _, part in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") then
            -- Scale kÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c lÃªn x3
            part.Size = part.Size * scale
            
            -- Äá»•i mÃ u Ä‘á»ƒ dá»… tháº¥y (mÃ u cam)
            part.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 165, 0)
            part.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
            
            -- ThÃªm Ã¡nh sÃ¡ng cho part lá»›n
            local light = Instance.new("PointLight")
            light.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 100)
            light.Range = 10
            light.Brightness = 1
            light.Parent = part
        end
    end
    
    -- Scale accessories
    for _, accessory in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
        if accessory:IsA("Accessory") then
            local handle = accessory:FindFirstChild("Handle")
            if handle and handle:IsA("BasePart") then
                handle.Size = handle.Size * scale
                handle.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 100)
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- TÄƒng tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ di chuyá»ƒn
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
        humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16 * (scale / 2)
        humanoid.JumpPower = 50 * (scale / 2)
        print("ðŸƒâ€â™‚ï¸ Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. humanoid.WalkSpeed)
    end
    
    print("âœ… ÄÃƒ BIáº¾N TO X" .. scale .. " THÃ€NH CÃ”NG!")
end

-- Nháº­n scale tá»« server
scaleRemote.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(action, player, scale)
    if action == "scale" then
        if player and player.Character then
            print("ðŸŽ¯ Äang scale " .. player.Name .. " x" .. scale)
            applyBigScale(player.Character, scale)
        end
    end
end)

-- HÃ€M CHÃNH - SCALE NGAY KHI EXECUTE
local function scaleImmediately()
    print("ðŸš€ Báº®T Äáº¦U BIáº¾N TO X" .. SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
    
    -- 1. Táº¡o server script
    createServerScript()
    
    -- 2. Scale báº£n thÃ¢n ngay
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if character then
        -- Scale local trÆ°á»›c cho nhanh
        applyBigScale(character, SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
        
        -- Gá»­i lÃªn server Ä‘á»ƒ má»i ngÆ°á»i tháº¥y
        scaleRemote:FireServer("scale", SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
        
        isScaled = true
    else
        print("â³ Äá»£i character load...")
        LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
        task.wait(1)
        character = LocalPlayer.Character
        applyBigScale(character, SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
        scaleRemote:FireServer("scale", SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
        isScaled = true
    end
    
    print("âœ¨ Báº N ÄÃƒ BIáº¾N THÃ€NH NGÆ¯á»œI KHá»”NG Lá»’ X" .. SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
end

-- CHáº Y NGAY KHI EXECUTE
scaleImmediately()

-- Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng scale khi respawn
LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(newCharacter)
    task.wait(2)  -- Äá»£i character load Ä‘áº§y Ä‘á»§
    if isScaled then
        print("ðŸ”„ Äang scale láº¡i khi respawn...")
        applyBigScale(newCharacter, SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
        scaleRemote:FireServer("scale", SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
    end
end)

-- PhÃ­m táº¯t (tÃ¹y chá»n)
game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
    if gameProcessed then return end
    
    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.R then
        -- R: Scale láº¡i
        print("ðŸ”„ Scale láº¡i x" .. SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
        local character = LocalPlayer.Character
        if character then
            applyBigScale(character, SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
            scaleRemote:FireServer("scale", SCALE_MULTIPLIER)
        end
    end
end)

print("ðŸ‘¥ Má»i ngÆ°á»i trong server Ä‘á»u tháº¥y")

     Callback = function()
       -- TOÃ€N Bá»˜ SCRIPT - CHáº Y á»ž CLIENT (Executor)
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local SoundService = game:GetService("SoundService")
local Lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")

local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

-- Config
local SOUND_ID = "rbxassetid://5943190023"
local IMAGE_ID = "rbxassetid://134973285396563"

print("ðŸŽµðŸŽ¨ Äang khá»Ÿi Ä‘á»™ng hiá»‡u á»©ng toÃ n server...")

-- ========== Táº O REMOTE EVENTS ==========
-- RemoteEvent cho Ã¢m nháº¡c
local musicRemote
if ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild("GlobalMusicRemote") then
    musicRemote = ReplicatedStorage.GlobalMusicRemote
else
    musicRemote = Instance.new("RemoteEvent")
    musicRemote.Name = "GlobalMusicRemote"

-- ========== Táº O SERVER SCRIPT Tá»° Äá»˜NG ==========
-- Táº¡o server script trong ServerScriptService
local function createServerScript()
    local serverScriptService = game:GetService("ServerScriptService")
    
    -- Kiá»ƒm tra xem server script Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i chÆ°a
    if serverScriptService:FindFirstChild("GlobalEffectsServer") then
        print("âœ… Server script Ä‘Ã£ tá»“n táº¡i")
        return
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o server script
    local script = Instance.new("Script")
    script.Name = "GlobalEffectsServer"
    
    -- Ná»™i dung server script
    script.Source = [[
        local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
        local musicRemote = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("GlobalMusicRemote")
        local textureRemote = ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("GlobalTextureRemote")
        
        print("ðŸŽµðŸŽ¨ Server Effects Script Ä‘Ã£ khá»Ÿi Ä‘á»™ng")
        
        -- Xá»­ lÃ½ sá»± kiá»‡n Ã¢m nháº¡c
        musicRemote.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, action, ...)
            if action == "play" then
                local soundId, volume, looped = ...
                print("ðŸŽµ PhÃ¡t nháº¡c toÃ n server: " .. soundId)
                musicRemote:FireAllClients("play", soundId, volume, looped)
                
            elseif action == "stop" then
                print("â¹ï¸ Dá»«ng nháº¡c toÃ n server")
                musicRemote:FireAllClients("stop")
                
            elseif action == "volume" then
                local volume = ...
                musicRemote:FireAllClients("volume", volume)
            end
        end)
        
        -- Xá»­ lÃ½ sá»± kiá»‡n texture
        textureRemote.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(player, action, textureId)
            if action == "skybox" then
                print("ðŸŒŒ Ãp dá»¥ng skybox: " .. textureId)
                textureRemote:FireAllClients("skybox", textureId)
                
            elseif action == "workspace" then
                print("ðŸ—ï¸ Ãp dá»¥ng texture workspace: " .. textureId)
                textureRemote:FireAllClients("workspace", textureId)
                
            elseif action == "player" then
                print("ðŸ‘¥ Ãp dá»¥ng texture players: " .. textureId)
                textureRemote:FireAllClients("player", textureId)
            end
        end)
        
        print("âœ… Server script sáºµn sÃ ng xá»­ lÃ½ events")
    ]]
    
    script.Parent = serverScriptService
    print("âœ… ÄÃ£ táº¡o server script tá»± Ä‘á»™ng")
end

-- ========== PHáº¦N Ã‚M THANH ==========
local globalSound = nil

local function playGlobalSound()
    -- Táº¡o sound local trÆ°á»›c
    globalSound = Instance.new("Sound")
    globalSound.SoundId = SOUND_ID
    globalSound.Name = "GlobalMusic"
    globalSound.Volume = 0.7
    globalSound.Looped = true
    globalSound.Parent = SoundService
    globalSound:Play()
    
    -- Gá»­i Ä‘áº¿n server
    musicRemote:FireServer("play", SOUND_ID, 0.7, true)
    
    print("ðŸ”Š Äang phÃ¡t nháº¡c: " .. SOUND_ID)
end

-- Nháº­n sá»± kiá»‡n tá»« server
musicRemote.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(action, ...)
    if action == "play" then
        local soundId, volume, looped = ...
        local sound = Instance.new("Sound")
        sound.SoundId = soundId
        sound.Name = "ServerMusic"
        sound.Volume = volume or 0.7
        sound.Looped = looped or true
        sound.Parent = SoundService
        sound:Play()
        print("ðŸŽµ Äang nghe nháº¡c tá»« server")
        
    elseif action == "stop" then
        for _, s in ipairs(SoundService:GetChildren()) do
            if s.Name == "ServerMusic" then
                s:Stop()
                s:Destroy()
            end
        end
        print("â¹ï¸ Nháº¡c Ä‘Ã£ dá»«ng")
        
    elseif action == "volume" then
        local volume = ...
        for _, s in ipairs(SoundService:GetChildren()) do
            if s.Name == "ServerMusic" then
                s.Volume = volume
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- ========== PHáº¦N TEXTURE ==========
local function applyTextureToPart(part)
    if not part:IsA("BasePart") then return end
    
    -- XÃ³a decal cÅ©
    for _, child in ipairs(part:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("Decal") then
            child:Destroy()
        end
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o decal má»›i
    local frontDecal = Instance.new("Decal")
    frontDecal.Texture = IMAGE_ID
    frontDecal.Face = Enum.NormalId.Front
    frontDecal.Parent = part
    
    local backDecal = Instance.new("Decal")
    backDecal.Texture = IMAGE_ID
    backDecal.Face = Enum.NormalId.Back
    backDecal.Parent = part
    
    part.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    part.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
end

-- Ãp dá»¥ng texture cho táº¥t cáº£ players
local function applyTextureToAllPlayers()
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player.Character then
            for _, part in ipairs(player.Character:GetChildren()) do
                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                    applyTextureToPart(part)
                end
            end
        end
    end
    print("ðŸ‘¥ ÄÃ£ Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture cho players")
end

-- Táº¡o skybox
local function createGlobalSkybox()
    local sky = Instance.new("Sky")
    sky.SkyboxBk = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxDn = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxFt = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxLf = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxRt = IMAGE_ID
    sky.SkyboxUp = IMAGE_ID
    sky.Parent = Lighting
    
    textureRemote:FireServer("skybox", IMAGE_ID)
    print("ðŸŒŒ ÄÃ£ táº¡o skybox")
end

-- Ãp dá»¥ng texture cho workspace
local function applyTextureToWorkspace()
    for _, obj in ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
        if obj:IsA("BasePart") and not obj:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
            applyTextureToPart(obj)
        end
    end
    textureRemote:FireServer("workspace", IMAGE_ID)
    print("ðŸ—ï¸ ÄÃ£ Ã¡p dá»¥ng texture workspace")
end

-- Nháº­n sá»± kiá»‡n texture tá»« server
textureRemote.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(action, textureId)
    if action == "skybox" then
        local sky = Instance.new("Sky")
        sky.SkyboxBk = textureId
        sky.SkyboxDn = textureId
        sky.SkyboxFt = textureId
        sky.SkyboxLf = textureId
        sky.SkyboxRt = textureId
        sky.SkyboxUp = textureId
        sky.Parent = Lighting
        
    elseif action == "workspace" then
        for _, obj in ipairs(Workspace:GetDescendants()) do
            if obj:IsA("BasePart") and not obj:IsDescendantOf(game.Players) then
                applyTextureToPart(obj)
            end
        end
        
    elseif action == "player" then
        applyTextureToAllPlayers()
    end
end)

    createGlobalSkybox()
    applyTextureToWorkspace()
    
    -- 4. Gá»­i sá»± kiá»‡n cho ngÆ°á»i khÃ¡c
    textureRemote:FireServer("player", IMAGE_ID)
    
    print("âœ¨ Má»i thá»© Ä‘Ã£ sáºµn sÃ ng!")

        globalSound:Stop()
        globalSound:Destroy()
        globalSound = nil
    end
    musicRemote:FireServer("stop")
    print("â¹ï¸ ÄÃ£ dá»«ng nháº¡c")

    local vol = math.clamp(volume, 0, 1)
    if globalSound then
        globalSound.Volume = vol
    end
    musicRemote:FireServer("volume", vol)
    print("ðŸŽšï¸ Volume: " .. vol)

        if globalSound then
            if globalSound.IsPlaying then
                globalSound:Pause()
                print("â¸ï¸ Táº¡m dá»«ng")
            else
                globalSound:Play()
                print("â–¶ï¸ Tiáº¿p tá»¥c")
            end
        end
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.S then
        stopGlobalSound()
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.R then
        print("ðŸ”„ Khá»Ÿi Ä‘á»™ng láº¡i...")
        stopGlobalSound()
        task.wait(0.5)
        startGlobalEffects()
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Up then
        if globalSound then
            setGlobalVolume(globalSound.Volume + 0.1)
        end
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Down then
        if globalSound then
            setGlobalVolume(globalSound.Volume - 0.1)
        end
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.M then
        if globalSound then
            if globalSound.Volume > 0 then
                globalSound.Volume = 0
                print("ðŸ”‡ Mute")
            else
                globalSound.Volume = 0.7
                print("ðŸ”Š Unmute")
            end
        end
    end
end)

       -- Script biáº¿n thÃ nh zombie ngay khi execute
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer
local character = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()

print("ðŸ§Ÿâ€â™‚ï¸ Äang biáº¿n thÃ nh zombie...")

-- áº¨n toÃ n bá»™ character cÅ©
for _, part in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
    if part:IsA("BasePart") then
        part.Transparency = 1
        part.CanCollide = false
    end
end

-- XÃ³a táº¥t cáº£ phá»¥ kiá»‡n
for _, item in ipairs(character:GetChildren()) do
    if item:IsA("Accessory") or item:IsA("Hat") then
        item:Destroy()
    end
end

-- Láº¥y HumanoidRootPart Ä‘á»ƒ gáº¯n zombie
local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
if not hrp then
    hrp = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
end

-- Táº¡o model zombie
local zombieModel = Instance.new("Model")
zombieModel.Name = "Zombie"

-- Táº¡o cÃ¡c bá»™ pháº­n zombie
local parts = {
    Torso = {size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 1), color = Color3.fromRGB(50, 150, 50), pos = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)},
    Head = {size = Vector3.new(2, 1.5, 2), color = Color3.fromRGB(40, 120, 40), pos = Vector3.new(0, 1.5, 0)},
    LeftArm = {size = Vector3.new(1, 2, 1), color = Color3.fromRGB(50, 150, 50), pos = Vector3.new(-1.5, 0, 0)},
    RightArm = {size = Vector3.new(1, 2, 1), color = Color3.fromRGB(50, 150, 50), pos = Vector3.new(1.5, 0, 0)},
    LeftLeg = {size = Vector3.new(1, 2, 1), color = Color3.fromRGB(50, 150, 50), pos = Vector3.new(-0.5, -1.5, 0)},
    RightLeg = {size = Vector3.new(1, 2, 1), color = Color3.fromRGB(50, 150, 50), pos = Vector3.new(0.5, -1.5, 0)}
}

local createdParts = {}

-- Táº¡o táº¥t cáº£ parts
for partName, data in pairs(parts) do
    local part = Instance.new("Part")
    part.Name = partName
    part.Size = data.size
    part.Color = data.color
    part.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
    part.Transparency = 0.2
    part.CanCollide = false
    part.Anchored = false
    part.Parent = zombieModel
    
    createdParts[partName] = part
end

-- Táº¡o Humanoid cho zombie
local zombieHumanoid = Instance.new("Humanoid")
zombieHumanoid.WalkSpeed = 12
zombieHumanoid.JumpPower = 30
zombieHumanoid.Parent = zombieModel

-- Gáº¯n cÃ¡c parts báº±ng Motor6D
local function createWeld(part0, part1, c0)
    local weld = Instance.new("Motor6D")
    weld.Name = part1.Name .. "Weld"
    weld.Part0 = part0
    weld.Part1 = part1
    weld.C0 = c0
    weld.Parent = part0
end

-- Torso lÃ  root part
local torso = createdParts.Torso
zombieModel.PrimaryPart = torso

-- Gáº¯n cÃ¡c parts vÃ o torso
createWeld(torso, createdParts.Head, CFrame.new(0, 1, 0))
createWeld(torso, createdParts.LeftArm, CFrame.new(-1.5, 0.5, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(45))) -- Tay trÃ¡i giÆ¡ lÃªn
createWeld(torso, createdParts.RightArm, CFrame.new(1.5, 0.5, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(-45))) -- Tay pháº£i giÆ¡ lÃªn
createWeld(torso, createdParts.LeftLeg, CFrame.new(-0.5, -1, 0))
createWeld(torso, createdParts.RightLeg, CFrame.new(0.5, -1, 0))

-- ThÃªm máº¯t Ä‘á»
local leftEye = Instance.new("Part")
leftEye.Name = "LeftEye"
leftEye.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball
leftEye.Size = Vector3.new(0.4, 0.4, 0.4)
leftEye.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
leftEye.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
leftEye.CanCollide = false
leftEye.Parent = createdParts.Head

local rightEye = Instance.new("Part")
rightEye.Name = "RightEye"
rightEye.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball
rightEye.Size = Vector3.new(0.4, 0.4, 0.4)
rightEye.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
rightEye.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
rightEye.CanCollide = false
rightEye.Parent = createdParts.Head

-- Gáº¯n máº¯t vÃ o Ä‘áº§u
local leftEyeWeld = Instance.new("Weld")
leftEyeWeld.Part0 = createdParts.Head
leftEyeWeld.Part1 = leftEye
leftEyeWeld.C0 = CFrame.new(-0.3, 0.2, 0.5)
leftEyeWeld.Parent = leftEye

local rightEyeWeld = Instance.new("Weld")
rightEyeWeld.Part0 = createdParts.Head
rightEyeWeld.Part1 = rightEye
rightEyeWeld.C0 = CFrame.new(0.3, 0.2, 0.5)
rightEyeWeld.Parent = rightEye

-- Ãnh sÃ¡ng tá»« máº¯t
local leftLight = Instance.new("PointLight")
leftLight.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
leftLight.Range = 10
leftLight.Brightness = 2
leftLight.Parent = leftEye

local rightLight = Instance.new("PointLight")

rightLight.Range = 10
rightLight.Brightness = 2

-- ThÃªm váº¿t thÆ°Æ¡ng
local wound = Instance.new("Part")
wound.Name = "Wound"
wound.Shape = Enum.PartType.Ball
wound.Size = Vector3.new(0.8, 0.8, 0.8)
wound.Color = Color3.fromRGB(150, 0, 0)
wound.Material = Enum.Material.Neon

wound.Parent = torso

local woundWeld = Instance.new("Weld")

-- Gáº¯n zombie vÃ o character
local zombieWeld = Instance.new("Weld")
zombieWeld.Part0 = hrp
zombieWeld.Part1 = torso
zombieWeld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 0, 0)
zombieWeld.Parent = torso

zombieModel.Parent = workspace

-- Hiá»‡u á»©ng tay giÆ¡ lÃªn xuá»‘ng
coroutine.wrap(function()
    while true do
        local leftArmWeld = torso:FindFirstChild("LeftArmWeld")
        local rightArmWeld = torso:FindFirstChild("RightArmWeld")
        
        if leftArmWeld and rightArmWeld then
            local wave = math.sin(tick() * 2) * 0.3
            leftArmWeld.C0 = CFrame.new(-1.5, 0.5 + wave, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(45))
            rightArmWeld.C0 = CFrame.new(1.5, 0.5 - wave, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, math.rad(-45))
        end
        
        -- Hiá»‡u á»©ng nháº¥p nhÃ¡y máº¯t
        leftLight.Brightness = 1.5 + math.sin(tick() * 5) * 0.5
        rightLight.Brightness = 1.5 + math.sin(tick() * 5 + 1) * 0.5
        
        task.wait(0.1)
    end
end)()

-- Ã‚m thanh zombie (tÃ¹y chá»n)
local sound = Instance.new("Sound")
sound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://911846469"
sound.Volume = 0.3
sound.Looped = true
sound.Parent = torso
sound:Play()

RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    if character and hrp then
        torso.Position = hrp.Position
    end
end)

AddButton(Tab0o, {
  	Name = "triá»‡u há»“i dummy",
     Callback = function()
       -- Script triá»‡u há»“i Dummy mÃ u tráº¯ng Äá»¨NG YÃŠN - cÃ³ thá»ƒ bá»‹ sÃ¡t thÆ°Æ¡ng
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local Workspace = game:GetService("Workspace")
local LocalPlayer = Players.LocalPlayer

print("ðŸ¤– Äang triá»‡u há»“i Dummy Ä‘á»©ng yÃªn...")

-- HÃ m táº¡o Dummy Äá»¨NG YÃŠN
local function spawnDummy()
    -- Vá»‹ trÃ­ spawn (trÆ°á»›c máº·t player)
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return end
    
    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return end
    
    local spawnPos = hrp.Position + hrp.CFrame.LookVector * 5
    
    -- Táº¡o model Dummy
    local dummy = Instance.new("Model")
    dummy.Name = "WhiteDummy"
    
    -- Táº¡o HumanoidRootPart (Cá» Äá»ŠNH)
    local rootPart = Instance.new("Part")
    rootPart.Name = "HumanoidRootPart"
    rootPart.Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 1)
    rootPart.Position = spawnPos
    rootPart.Anchored = true  -- QUAN TRá»ŒNG: Äá»¨NG YÃŠN
    rootPart.CanCollide = true
    rootPart.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    rootPart.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
    rootPart.Parent = dummy
    
    -- Táº¡o cÃ¡c bá»™ pháº­n (táº¥t cáº£ Ä‘á»u anchored)
    local parts = {
        {Name = "Head", Size = Vector3.new(2, 1.5, 2), Position = Vector3.new(0, 1.5, 0)},
        {Name = "Torso", Size = Vector3.new(2, 2, 1), Position = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)},
        {Name = "LeftArm", Size = Vector3.new(1, 2, 1), Position = Vector3.new(-1.5, 0, 0)},
        {Name = "RightArm", Size = Vector3.new(1, 2, 1), Position = Vector3.new(1.5, 0, 0)},
        {Name = "LeftLeg", Size = Vector3.new(1, 2, 1), Position = Vector3.new(-0.5, -1.5, 0)},
        {Name = "RightLeg", Size = Vector3.new(1, 2, 1), Position = Vector3.new(0.5, -1.5, 0)}
    }
    
    local createdParts = {}
    
    -- Táº¡o táº¥t cáº£ parts vá»›i Anchored = true
    for _, partData in ipairs(parts) do
        local part = Instance.new("Part")
        part.Name = partData.Name
        part.Size = partData.Size
        part.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
        part.Material = Enum.Material.Plastic
        part.CanCollide = true
        part.Anchored = true  -- QUAN TRá»ŒNG: Äá»¨NG YÃŠN
        part.Parent = dummy
        
        createdParts[partData.Name] = part
    end
    
    -- Táº¡o Humanoid nhÆ°ng DISABLE di chuyá»ƒn
    local humanoid = Instance.new("Humanoid")
    humanoid.Name = "DummyHumanoid"
    humanoid.MaxHealth = 100
    humanoid.Health = 100
    humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
    humanoid.JumpPower = 0
    humanoid.PlatformStand = true  -- KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ di chuyá»ƒn
    humanoid.AutoRotate = false    -- KhÃ´ng tá»± xoay
    humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = Enum.HumanoidDisplayDistanceType.None
    humanoid.Parent = dummy
    
    -- Thanh mÃ¡u
    local healthDisplay = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
    healthDisplay.Name = "HealthDisplay"
    healthDisplay.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 30)
    healthDisplay.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
    healthDisplay.AlwaysOnTop = true
    healthDisplay.Adornee = rootPart
    
    local healthBar = Instance.new("Frame")
    healthBar.Name = "HealthBar"
    healthBar.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.5, 0)
    healthBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
    healthBar.BorderSizePixel = 0
    healthBar.Parent = healthDisplay
    
    local healthText = Instance.new("TextLabel")
    healthText.Name = "HealthText"
    healthText.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 0.5, 0)
    healthText.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0.5, 0)
    healthText.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    healthText.Text = "100/100 HP"
    healthText.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255)
    healthText.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
    healthText.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    healthText.TextSize = 14
    healthText.Parent = healthDisplay
    
    healthDisplay.Parent = rootPart
    
    -- Gáº¯n cÃ¡c parts báº±ng Weld (Ä‘á»ƒ khÃ´ng bá»‹ rÆ¡i ra)
    local function createWeld(part0, part1, offset)
        local weld = Instance.new("Weld")
        weld.Part0 = part0
        weld.Part1 = part1
        weld.C0 = offset
        weld.Parent = part1
    end
    
    -- Gáº¯n cÃ¡c parts vÃ o rootPart
    createWeld(rootPart, createdParts.Torso, CFrame.new(0, 0, 0))
    createWeld(rootPart, createdParts.Head, CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0))
    createWeld(rootPart, createdParts.LeftArm, CFrame.new(-1.5, 0, 0))
    createWeld(rootPart, createdParts.RightArm, CFrame.new(1.5, 0, 0))
    createWeld(rootPart, createdParts.LeftLeg, CFrame.new(-0.5, -1.5, 0))
    createWeld(rootPart, createdParts.RightLeg, CFrame.new(0.5, -1.5, 0))
    
    -- Äáº·t táº¥t cáº£ parts vÃ o Ä‘Ãºng vá»‹ trÃ­
    for partName, part in pairs(createdParts) do
        local offset
        if partName == "Torso" then
            offset = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
        elseif partName == "Head" then
            offset = Vector3.new(0, 1.5, 0)
        elseif partName == "LeftArm" then
            offset = Vector3.new(-1.5, 0, 0)
        elseif partName == "RightArm" then
            offset = Vector3.new(1.5, 0, 0)
        elseif partName == "LeftLeg" then
            offset = Vector3.new(-0.5, -1.5, 0)
        elseif partName == "RightLeg" then
            offset = Vector3.new(0.5, -1.5, 0)
        end
        
        if offset then
            part.Position = rootPart.Position + offset
        end
    end
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t thanh mÃ¡u
    humanoid.HealthChanged:Connect(function()
        local healthPercent = humanoid.Health / humanoid.MaxHealth
        
        healthBar.Size = UDim2.new(healthPercent, 0, 0.5, 0)
        
        if healthPercent > 0.5 then
            healthBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0)
        elseif healthPercent > 0.25 then
            healthBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 0)
        else
            healthBar.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
        end
        
        healthText.Text = math.floor(humanoid.Health) .. "/" .. humanoid.MaxHealth .. " HP"
    end)
    
    -- Hiá»‡u á»©ng khi cháº¿t
    humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
        print("ðŸ’€ Dummy Ä‘Ã£ cháº¿t!")
        
        -- LÃ m trong suá»‘t dáº§n
        for i = 0, 1, 0.1 do
            for _, part in ipairs(dummy:GetChildren()) do
                if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                    part.Transparency = i
                end
            end
            task.wait(0.05)
        end
        
        task.wait(1)
        if dummy and dummy.Parent then
            dummy:Destroy()
        end
    end)
    
    -- Headshot damage
    local head = createdParts.Head
    head.Touched:Connect(function(hit)
        local tool = hit.Parent
        if tool and tool:IsA("Tool") then
            humanoid:TakeDamage(25)
            print("ðŸŽ¯ Headshot! -25 HP")
        end
    end)
    
    -- Äáº·t vÃ o workspace
    dummy.Parent = Workspace
    
    print("âœ… ÄÃ£ triá»‡u há»“i Dummy Äá»¨NG YÃŠN!")
    print("ðŸ“ Vá»‹ trÃ­ cá»‘ Ä‘á»‹nh")
    print("â¤ï¸ MÃ¡u: 100/100")
    
    return dummy
end

-- Triá»‡u há»“i ngay khi execute
spawnDummy()

-- Äiá»u khiá»ƒn
game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
    if not gameProcessed and input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.F then
        spawnDummy()
    end
    
    if not gameProcessed and input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.G then
        for _, obj in ipairs(Workspace:GetChildren()) do
            if obj.Name == "Dummy" then
                obj:Destroy()
            end
        end
        print("ðŸ§¹ ÄÃ£ xÃ³a táº¥t cáº£ Dummy")
    end
end)

print("=== DUMMY SPAWNER - Äá»¨NG YÃŠN ===")
print("ðŸ¤– Dummy Ä‘á»©ng yÃªn - khÃ´ng di chuyá»ƒn")
print("ðŸŽ® Äiá»u khiá»ƒn:")
print("   ðŸ…µ F: Triá»‡u há»“i thÃªm Dummy")
print("   ðŸ…¶ G: XÃ³a táº¥t cáº£ Dummy")
print("âš”ï¸ TÃ­nh nÄƒng:")
print("   - Anchored = true (khÃ´ng di chuyá»ƒn)")
print("   - PlatformStand = true")
print("   - WalkSpeed = 0")
print("   - CÃ³ thá»ƒ bá»‹ damage")
print("   - Headshot x2.5 damage")
  end
})
