-- HÃ m tÃ¬m ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i
local function findPlayerByName(name)
    local targetPlayer = nil
    
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if string.lower(player.Name) == string.lower(name) or 
           string.lower(player.DisplayName) == string.lower(name) then
            targetPlayer = player
            break
        end
    end
    
    return targetPlayer
end

-- HÃ m teleport
local function teleportToPlayer(playerName)
    if playerName == "" or playerName == "Nháº­p tÃªn ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i..." then
        StatusLabel.Text = "nháº­p tÃªn"
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 0)
        return
    end
    
    local targetPlayer = findPlayerByName(playerName)
    
    if not targetPlayer then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Ä‘Ã©o tÃ¬m tháº¥y: " .. playerName
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        return
    end
    
    if not targetPlayer.Character then
        StatusLabel.Text = "NgÆ°á»i chÆ¡i chÆ°a cÃ³ character"
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        return
    end
    
    local targetHRP = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not targetHRP then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Ä‘Ã©o tÃ¬m tháº¥y vá»‹ trÃ­"
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        return
    end
    
    -- Teleport
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then
        StatusLabel.Text = "NhÃ¢n váº­t cá»§a mÃ y chx cÃ³"
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        return
    end
    
    local myHRP = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not myHRP then
        StatusLabel.Text = "ÄÃ©o tÃ¬m tháº¥y vá»‹ trÃ­ cá»§a báº¡n"
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        return
    end
    
    -- Thá»±c hiá»‡n teleport
    myHRP.CFrame = targetHRP.CFrame + Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)  -- Teleport phÃ­a trÃªn 1 chÃºt
    
    StatusLabel.Text = "ÄÃ£ tp Ä‘áº¿n: " .. targetPlayer.Name
    StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
    
    print("ðŸš€ ÄÃ£ teleport Ä‘áº¿n " .. targetPlayer.Name)
    
    -- Reset sau 2 giÃ¢y
    task.wait(2)
    StatusLabel.Text = "Sáºµn sÃ ng..."
    StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
end

-- Sá»± kiá»‡n nÃºt teleport

    local playerName = TextBox.Text
    teleportToPlayer(playerName)
end)

    if enterPressed then
        local playerName = TextBox.Text
        teleportToPlayer(playerName)
    end
end)

-- Auto-complete khi gÃµ
TextBox:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Text"):Connect(function()
    local text = TextBox.Text
    if text == "" then return end
    
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player ~= LocalPlayer then
            local nameLower = string.lower(player.Name)
            local displayLower = string.lower(player.DisplayName)
            local inputLower = string.lower(text)
            
            if string.sub(nameLower, 1, #inputLower) == inputLower or
               string.sub(displayLower, 1, #inputLower) == inputLower then
                -- CÃ³ thá»ƒ thÃªm auto-complete á»Ÿ Ä‘Ã¢y
                break
            end
        end
    end
end)

-- Danh sÃ¡ch players khi focus vÃ o textbox

    local playersList = ""
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player ~= LocalPlayer then
            playersList = playersList .. player.Name .. " | "
        end
    end
    
    if playersList ~= "" then
        StatusLabel.Text = "NgÆ°á»i chÆ¡i: " .. string.sub(playersList, 1, -3)
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 255)
    end
end)

TextBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
    StatusLabel.Text = "Sáºµn sÃ ng..."
    StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
end)

            print("ðŸ“± ÄÃ£ hiá»‡n GUI Teleport")
        else
            print("ðŸ“± ÄÃ£ áº©n GUI Teleport")
        end
    end
end)

-- HÃ m tÃ¬m ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i
local function findPlayerByName(name)
    if name == "" then return nil end
    
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player ~= LocalPlayer then
            if string.lower(player.Name) == string.lower(name) or 
               string.lower(player.DisplayName) == string.lower(name) then
                return player
            end
        end
    end
    
    return nil
end

-- HÃ m báº­t NoClip (xuyÃªn tÆ°á»ng)
local function enableNoClip(character)
    for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") then
            part.CanCollide = false
        end
    end
end

-- HÃ m báº­t Ultra Fly Mode
local function enableUltraFly()
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return end
    
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    
    if not humanoid or not hrp then return end
    
    -- Báº­t NoClip
    enableNoClip(character)
    
    -- Táº¯t trá»ng lá»±c
    humanoid.PlatformStand = true
    
    -- Táº¡o BodyVelocity siÃªu máº¡nh
    if bodyVelocity then bodyVelocity:Destroy() end
    
    bodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
    bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    bodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(40000, 40000, 40000)  -- Lá»±c cá»±c máº¡nh
    bodyVelocity.P = 5000  -- P cao Ä‘á»ƒ pháº£n á»©ng nhanh
    bodyVelocity.Parent = hrp
    
    -- Táº¡o BodyGyro siÃªu nhanh
    if bodyGyro then bodyGyro:Destroy() end
    
    bodyGyro = Instance.new("BodyGyro")
    bodyGyro.MaxTorque = Vector3.new(40000, 40000, 40000)
    bodyGyro.P = 5000
    bodyGyro.D = 500
    bodyGyro.CFrame = hrp.CFrame
    bodyGyro.Parent = hrp
    
    print("ðŸš€ ÄÃ£ báº­t ULTRA FLY + NOClip")
end

-- HÃ m táº¯t Ultra Fly
local function disableUltraFly()
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return end
    
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
    
    if humanoid then
        humanoid.PlatformStand = false
    end
    
    -- Báº­t láº¡i Collide
    for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") then
            part.CanCollide = true
        end
    end
    
    if bodyVelocity then
        bodyVelocity:Destroy()
        bodyVelocity = nil
    end
    
    if bodyGyro then
        bodyGyro:Destroy()
        bodyGyro = nil
    end
    
    print("ðŸš€ ÄÃ£ táº¯t ULTRA FLY")
end

-- HÃ m bay SIÃŠU Tá»C Ä‘áº¿n ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i
local function ultraFollowPlayer()
    if not isFollowing or not targetPlayer then return end
    
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return end
    
    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp or not bodyVelocity then return end
    
    -- Kiá»ƒm tra target
    if not targetPlayer or not targetPlayer.Parent or not targetPlayer.Character then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Lá»—i"
        stopFollowing()
        return
    end
    
    local targetHRP = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not targetHRP then return end
    
    -- TÃ­nh vector SIÃŠU Tá»C tháº³ng Ä‘áº¿n target
    local direction = (targetHRP.Position - hrp.Position)
    local distance = direction.Magnitude
    
    -- KHÃ”NG bay vÃ²ng quanh - bay tháº³ng 100%
    if direction.Magnitude > 0 then
        direction = direction.Unit * followSpeed
    end
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng velocity SIÃŠU Tá»C
    bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(direction.X, direction.Y, direction.Z)
    
    -- Xoay NHANH vá» hÆ°á»›ng target
    if bodyGyro then
        bodyGyro.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position, targetHRP.Position)
    end
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t status
    StatusLabel.Text = "Äang bay theo: " .. targetPlayer.Name .. " (" .. math.floor(distance) .. " studs)"
end

-- Báº¯t Ä‘áº§u theo dÃµi SIÃŠU Tá»C
local function startUltraFollowing()
    local playerName = NameBox.Text
    targetPlayer = findPlayerByName(playerName)
    
    if not targetPlayer then
        StatusLabel.Text = "ÄÃ©o tÃ¬m tháº¥y: " .. playerName
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        return
    end
    
    if not targetPlayer.Character then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Target chÆ°a cÃ³ character"
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        return
    end
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ tá»« textbox
    local newSpeed = tonumber(SpeedBox.Text)
    if newSpeed and newSpeed >= 10 and newSpeed <= 500 then
        followSpeed = newSpeed
        SpeedLabel.Text = "Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. followSpeed
        SpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
    else
        SpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        StatusLabel.Text = "Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ tá»« 10-500"
        return
    end
    
    -- Báº­t Ultra Fly
    enableUltraFly()
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t tráº¡ng thÃ¡i
    isFollowing = true
    FollowButton.Text = "Dá»ªNG BAY"
    FollowButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
    
    StatusLabel.Text = "Äang bay theo: " .. targetPlayer.Name
    StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
    
    print("ðŸŽ¯ Báº¯t Ä‘áº§u ULTRA FOLLOW: " .. targetPlayer.Name .. " | Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. followSpeed)
end

-- Dá»«ng theo dÃµi
local function stopFollowing()
    isFollowing = false
    targetPlayer = nil
    
    FollowButton.Text = "Báº®T Äáº¦U THEO"
    FollowButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(0, 200, 100)
    
    StatusLabel.Text = "ÄÃ£ dá»«ng theo dÃµi"
    StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200)
    
    -- Táº¯t Ultra Fly
    disableUltraFly()
    
    print("ÄÃ£ dá»«ng ULTRA FOLLOW")
end

-- Toggle follow
local function toggleFollow()
    if isFollowing then
        stopFollowing()
    else
        startUltraFollowing()
    end
end

-- Sá»± kiá»‡n nÃºt
FollowButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(toggleFollow)

-- Cáº­p nháº­t ULTRA FOLLOW má»—i frame
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    if isFollowing and targetPlayer then
        ultraFollowPlayer()
    end
end)

-- Xá»­ lÃ½ SpeedBox
SpeedBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
    local newSpeed = tonumber(SpeedBox.Text)
    if newSpeed and newSpeed >= 10 and newSpeed <= 500 then
        followSpeed = newSpeed
        SpeedLabel.Text = "Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. followSpeed
        SpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
        print("Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ má»›i: " .. followSpeed)
    else
        SpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        SpeedBox.Text = tostring(followSpeed)
    end
end)

-- Nháº¥n Enter Ä‘á»ƒ báº¯t Ä‘áº§u/dá»«ng
NameBox.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
    if enterPressed and not isFollowing then
        startUltraFollowing()
    end
end)

-- PhÃ­m táº¯t SIÃŠU Tá»C
UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
    if gameProcessed then return end
    
    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.H then
        -- áº¨n/hiá»‡n GUI
        MainFrame.Visible = not MainFrame.Visible
        print(MainFrame.Visible and "ðŸ“± Hiá»‡n GUI" or "ðŸ“± áº¨n GUI")
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Escape then
        -- ThoÃ¡t follow khi nháº¥n ESC
        if isFollowing then
            stopFollowing()
        end
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.PageUp then
        -- TÄƒng tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ nhanh
        if followSpeed < 490 then
            followSpeed = followSpeed + 10
            SpeedBox.Text = tostring(followSpeed)
            SpeedLabel.Text = "Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. followSpeed
            print("ðŸ“ˆ Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. followSpeed)
        end
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.PageDown then
        -- Giáº£m tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ nhanh
        if followSpeed > 20 then
            followSpeed = followSpeed - 10
            SpeedBox.Text = tostring(followSpeed)
            SpeedLabel.Text = "Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. followSpeed
            print("ðŸ“‰ Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. followSpeed)
        end
    end
end)

-- Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng báº­t láº¡i khi respawn
LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
    if isFollowing then
        task.wait(1)
        enableUltraFly()
        print("ðŸ”„ Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng báº­t láº¡i ULTRA FLY khi respawn")
    end
end)

LocalPlayer.CharacterRemoving:Connect(function()
    if isFollowing then
        stopFollowing()
    end
end)

-- Auto-focus
NameBox.Focused:Connect(function()
    local playersList = ""
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player ~= LocalPlayer then
            playersList = playersList .. player.Name .. " | "
        end
    end
    
    if playersList ~= "" then
        StatusLabel.Text = "CÃ³ thá»ƒ theo: " .. string.sub(playersList, 1, -3)
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 255)
    end
end)

NameBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
    if not isFollowing then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Äang chá»..."
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 255)
    end
end)

print("âœ… ÄÃ£ táº¡o GUI ULTRA FOLLOW SIÃŠU Tá»C!")
print("ðŸš€ TÃ­nh nÄƒng:")
print("   - Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ bay: 100 (cÃ³ thá»ƒ chá»‰nh 10-500)")
print("   - NoClip: XuyÃªn tÆ°á»ng khi bay")
print("   - Bay tháº³ng 100%: KhÃ´ng bay vÃ²ng quanh")
print("   - BodyVelocity máº¡nh: Bay siÃªu nhanh")
print("ðŸŽ® Äiá»u khiá»ƒn:")
print("   ðŸ–±ï¸ Click nÃºt: Báº­t/táº¯t follow")
print("   â†©ï¸ Enter trong NameBox: Báº¯t Ä‘áº§u follow")
print("   ðŸ“„ Page Up/Down: TÄƒng/giáº£m tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ nhanh")
print("   ðŸ…· H: áº¨n/hiá»‡n GUI")
print("   âŽ‹ ESC: ThoÃ¡t follow")

-- Khá»Ÿi táº¡o
StatusLabel.Text = "Äang chá»"
SpeedLabel.Text = "Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. followSpeed
  end
})

-- HÃ m tÃ¬m ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i
local function findPlayerByName(name)
    if name == "" then return nil end
    
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player ~= LocalPlayer then
            if string.lower(player.Name) == string.lower(name) or 
               string.lower(player.DisplayName) == string.lower(name) then
                return player
            end
        end
    end
    
    return nil
end

-- HÃ m báº­t NoClip (FIXED - khÃ´ng dÃ¹ng BodyGyro)
local function enableNoClip(character)
    if not character then return end
    
    -- Báº­t NoClip cho táº¥t cáº£ parts
    for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") then
            part.CanCollide = false
        end
    end
    
    -- Báº­t PlatformStand Ä‘á»ƒ bay
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
        humanoid.PlatformStand = true
    end
end

-- HÃ m báº­t Orbit Fly Mode (FIXED)
local function enableOrbitFly()
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return end
    
    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp then return end
    
    -- Báº­t NoClip
    enableNoClip(character)
    
    -- Táº¡o BodyVelocity (khÃ´ng dÃ¹ng BodyGyro Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh káº¹t)
    if bodyVelocity then 
        bodyVelocity:Destroy() 
        bodyVelocity = nil
    end
    
    bodyVelocity = Instance.new("BodyVelocity")
    bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    bodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.new(10000, 10000, 10000)
    bodyVelocity.P = 1250  -- P tháº¥p hÆ¡n Ä‘á»ƒ mÆ°á»£t hÆ¡n
    bodyVelocity.Parent = hrp
    
    print("Da bat ORBIT FLY + NoClip (khong co BodyGyro)")
end

-- HÃ m táº¯t Orbit Fly
local function disableOrbitFly()
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return end
    
    local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
    
    if humanoid then
        humanoid.PlatformStand = false
    end
    
    -- Báº­t láº¡i Collide
    for _, part in ipairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
        if part:IsA("BasePart") then
            part.CanCollide = true
        end
    end
    
    if bodyVelocity then
        bodyVelocity:Destroy()
        bodyVelocity = nil
    end
    
    print("Da tat ORBIT FLY")
end

-- HÃ m bay vÃ²ng quanh ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i (FIXED - khÃ´ng káº¹t)
local function orbitFollowPlayer()
    if not isFollowing or not targetPlayer then return end
    
    local character = LocalPlayer.Character
    if not character then return end
    
    local hrp = character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not hrp or not bodyVelocity then return end
    
    -- Kiá»ƒm tra target
    if not targetPlayer or not targetPlayer.Parent or not targetPlayer.Character then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Mat ket noi voi target"
        stopFollowing()
        return
    end
    
    local targetHRP = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
    if not targetHRP then return end
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t gÃ³c quay
    orbitAngle = orbitAngle + (orbitSpeed * 0.1)
    
    -- TÃ­nh toÃ¡n vá»‹ trÃ­ bay vÃ²ng quanh
    local offsetX = math.cos(orbitAngle) * orbitRadius
    local offsetZ = math.sin(orbitAngle) * orbitRadius
    local offsetY = math.sin(orbitAngle * 2) * 3  -- Bay lÃªn xuá»‘ng nháº¹
    
    -- Vá»‹ trÃ­ má»¥c tiÃªu
    local targetPosition = targetHRP.Position + Vector3.new(offsetX, offsetY + 2, offsetZ)
    
    -- TÃ­nh vector Ä‘áº¿n vá»‹ trÃ­
    local direction = (targetPosition - hrp.Position)
    local distance = direction.Magnitude
    
    -- Ãp dá»¥ng velocity mÆ°á»£t mÃ 
    if distance > 2 then
        local speedMultiplier = math.min(followSpeed, distance * 2)  -- Giáº£m tá»‘c khi gáº§n
        if direction.Magnitude > 0 then
            direction = direction.Unit * speedMultiplier
        end
        
        bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(direction.X, direction.Y, direction.Z)
    else
        -- Giá»¯ nguyÃªn vá»‹ trÃ­ khi Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘áº¿n gáº§n
        bodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
    end
    
    -- Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng xoay nhÃ¬n vá» target (mÆ°á»£t hÆ¡n)
    local lookVector = (targetHRP.Position - hrp.Position).Unit
    hrp.CFrame = CFrame.new(hrp.Position, hrp.Position + lookVector)
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t status
    StatusLabel.Text = "Dang bay vong quanh: " .. targetPlayer.Name .. 
                      "\nBan kinh: " .. orbitRadius .. 
                      " | Khoang cach: " .. math.floor(distance) .. " studs"
end

-- Báº¯t Ä‘áº§u bay vÃ²ng quanh
local function startOrbitFollowing()
    local playerName = NameBox.Text
    targetPlayer = findPlayerByName(playerName)
    
    if not targetPlayer then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Khong tim thay: " .. playerName
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        return
    end
    
    if not targetPlayer.Character then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Target chua co character"
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        return
    end
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t tá»‘c Ä‘á»™
    local newSpeed = tonumber(SpeedBox.Text)
    if newSpeed and newSpeed >= 10 and newSpeed <= 100 then
        followSpeed = newSpeed
        SpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
    else
        SpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        StatusLabel.Text = "Toc do phai tu 10-100"
        return
    end
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t bÃ¡n kÃ­nh
    local newRadius = tonumber(RadiusBox.Text)
    if newRadius and newRadius >= 5 and newRadius <= 30 then
        orbitRadius = newRadius
        RadiusBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 200, 255)
    else
        RadiusBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        StatusLabel.Text = "Ban kinh phai tu 5-30"
        return
    end
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t tá»‘c Ä‘á»™ bay vÃ²ng
    local newOrbitSpeed = tonumber(OrbitSpeedBox.Text)
    if newOrbitSpeed and newOrbitSpeed >= 0.5 and newOrbitSpeed <= 3 then
        orbitSpeed = newOrbitSpeed
        OrbitSpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 100)
    else
        OrbitSpeedBox.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
        StatusLabel.Text = "Toc do bay vong phai tu 0.5-3"
        return
    end
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t labels
    SpeedLabel.Text = "Toc do: " .. followSpeed .. " | Ban kinh: " .. orbitRadius
    OrbitLabel.Text = "Toc do bay vong: " .. orbitSpeed
    
    -- Reset gÃ³c quay
    orbitAngle = 0
    
    -- Báº­t Orbit Fly
    enableOrbitFly()
    
    -- Cáº­p nháº­t tráº¡ng thÃ¡i
    isFollowing = true
    FollowButton.Text = "DUNG ORBIT"
    FollowButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
    
    StatusLabel.Text = "Dang bay vong quanh: " .. targetPlayer.Name
    StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
    
    print("Bat dau ORBIT FOLLOW: " .. targetPlayer.Name)
end

-- Dá»«ng bay vÃ²ng quanh
local function stopFollowing()
    isFollowing = false
    targetPlayer = nil
    orbitAngle = 0
    
    FollowButton.Text = "BAT DAU ORBIT"
    FollowButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 0, 150)
    
    StatusLabel.Text = "Nhap ten nguoi choi va dieu chinh thong so..."
    StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 255)
    
    -- Táº¯t Orbit Fly
    disableOrbitFly()
    
    print("Da dung ORBIT FOLLOW")
end

-- Toggle follow
FollowButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
    if isFollowing then
        stopFollowing()
    else
        startOrbitFollowing()
    end
end)

-- Cáº­p nháº­t orbit má»—i frame
RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
    if isFollowing and targetPlayer then
        orbitFollowPlayer()
    end
end)

-- Xá»­ lÃ½ cÃ¡c textbox
local function validateTextBox(box, min, max, defaultColor)
    box.FocusLost:Connect(function()
        local value = tonumber(box.Text)
        if value and value >= min and value <= max then
            box.TextColor3 = defaultColor
            return true
        else
            box.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
            box.Text = tostring(min)
            return false
        end
    end)
end

-- Ãp dá»¥ng validation
validateTextBox(SpeedBox, 10, 100, Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100))
validateTextBox(RadiusBox, 5, 30, Color3.fromRGB(100, 200, 255))
validateTextBox(OrbitSpeedBox, 0.5, 3, Color3.fromRGB(255, 200, 100))

-- Nháº¥n Enter trong NameBox Ä‘á»ƒ báº¯t Ä‘áº§u
NameBox.FocusLost:Connect(function(enterPressed)
    if enterPressed and not isFollowing then
        startOrbitFollowing()
    end
end)

-- PhÃ­m táº¯t
UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
    if gameProcessed then return end
    
    if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.H then
        MainFrame.Visible = not MainFrame.Visible
        print(MainFrame.Visible and "Hien GUI" or "An GUI")
        
    elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Escape then
        if isFollowing then
            stopFollowing()
        end
    end
end)

-- Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng báº­t láº¡i khi respawn
LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
    if isFollowing then
        task.wait(1)
        enableOrbitFly()
    end
end)

LocalPlayer.CharacterRemoving:Connect(function()
    if isFollowing then
        stopFollowing()
    end
end)

-- Auto-focus
NameBox.Focused:Connect(function()
    local playersList = ""
    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
        if player ~= LocalPlayer then
            playersList = playersList .. player.Name .. " | "
        end
    end
    
    if playersList ~= "" then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Co the theo: " .. string.sub(playersList, 1, -3)
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 255)
    end
end)

NameBox.FocusLost:Connect(function()
    if not isFollowing then
        StatusLabel.Text = "Nhap ten nguoi choi va dieu chinh thong so..."
        StatusLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 255)
    end
end)

    end

AddButton(Tab0o, {
    Name = "Táº¯t thanh chat",
    Callback = function()
      -- Script táº¯t thanh chat
local StarterGui = game:GetService("StarterGui")

print("ðŸ”‡ Äang táº¯t thanh chat...")

-- Pháº§n 1: Táº¯t CoreGui Chat
local function disableCoreGuiChat()
    local success = pcall(function()
        StarterGui:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Chat, false)
        print("âœ… ÄÃ£ táº¯t CoreGui Chat")
    end)
    
    if not success then
        print("âš ï¸ KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ táº¯t CoreGui Chat báº±ng phÆ°Æ¡ng phÃ¡p 1")
    end
end

-- Pháº§n 2: TÃ¬m vÃ  áº©n ChatFrame
local function hideChatFrame()
    local playerGui = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
    
    -- TÃ¬m ChatFrame
    local chatFrame = playerGui:FindFirstChild("Chat")
    if chatFrame then
        chatFrame.Enabled = false
        print("âœ… ÄÃ£ tÃ¬m tháº¥y vÃ  táº¯t ChatFrame")
    else
        print("âš ï¸ KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y ChatFrame")
    end
    
    -- TÃ¬m ChatBar
    local chatBar = playerGui:FindFirstChild("ChatBar")
    if chatBar then
        chatBar.Enabled = false
        print("âœ… ÄÃ£ tÃ¬m tháº¥y vÃ  táº¯t ChatBar")
    end
end

-- Pháº§n 3: áº¨n táº¥t cáº£ UI cá»§a chat
local function hideAllChatUI()
    local playerGui = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
    
    -- TÃ¬m táº¥t cáº£ chat-related GUI
    for _, gui in ipairs(playerGui:GetDescendants()) do
        if gui:IsA("GuiObject") then
            local name = gui.Name:lower()
            
            if name:find("chat") or 
               name:find("message") or 
               name:find("textchannel") or
               name:find("textbox") then
               
                gui.Visible = false
                gui.Active = false
            end
        end
    end
    
    print("âœ… ÄÃ£ áº©n táº¥t cáº£ chat-related UI")
end

-- Pháº§n 4: XÃ³a ChatScript
local function removeChatScripts()
    -- TÃ¬m trong PlayerScripts
    local playerScripts = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerScripts")
    
    for _, script in ipairs(playerScripts:GetDescendants()) do
        if script:IsA("LocalScript") then
            local name = script.Name:lower()
            
            if name:find("chat") or name:find("message") then
                script:Destroy()
                print("âœ… ÄÃ£ xÃ³a Chat Script: " .. script.Name)
            end
        end
    end
end

-- Pháº§n 5: NgÄƒn chat má»›i Ä‘Æ°á»£c táº¡o
local function preventNewChat()
    local playerGui = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
    
    -- Theo dÃµi khi cÃ³ GUI má»›i Ä‘Æ°á»£c thÃªm
    playerGui.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(descendant)
        if descendant:IsA("GuiObject") then
            local name = descendant.Name:lower()
            
            if name:find("chat") or 
               name:find("message") or 
               name:find("textchannel") then
               
                task.wait(0.1)  -- Äá»£i má»™t chÃºt
                if descendant:IsA("GuiObject") then
                    descendant.Visible = false
                    descendant.Active = false
                    print("ðŸ›¡ï¸ ÄÃ£ cháº·n chat GUI má»›i: " .. descendant.Name)
                end
            end
        end
    end)
    
    print("âœ… ÄÃ£ báº­t cháº¿ Ä‘á»™ cháº·n chat má»›i")
end

-- Pháº§n 6: Táº¡o GUI Ä‘á»ƒ báº­t/táº¯t chat
local function createToggleGUI()
    local screenGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
    screenGui.Name = "ChatToggleGUI"
    screenGui.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")
    
    local frame = Instance.new("Frame")
    frame.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 40)
    frame.Position = UDim2.new(0, 20, 0, 100)
    frame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(40, 40, 40)
    frame.BackgroundTransparency = 0.3
    frame.BorderSizePixel = 0
    frame.Parent = screenGui
    
    local button = Instance.new("TextButton")
    button.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
    button.BackgroundTransparency = 1
    button.Text = "Chat: OFF"
    button.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
    button.Font = Enum.Font.GothamBold
    button.TextSize = 14
    button.Parent = frame
    
    local chatEnabled = false
    
    button.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        chatEnabled = not chatEnabled
        
        if chatEnabled then
            -- Báº­t chat
            StarterGui:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Chat, true)
            button.Text = "Chat: ON"
            button.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(100, 255, 100)
            print("ðŸ’¬ ÄÃ£ báº­t chat")
        else
            -- Táº¯t chat
            StarterGui:SetCoreGuiEnabled(Enum.CoreGuiType.Chat, false)
            button.Text = "Chat: OFF"
            button.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100)
            
            -- áº¨n láº¡i táº¥t cáº£ chat UI
            hideChatFrame()
            hideAllChatUI()
            
            print("ðŸ”‡ ÄÃ£ táº¯t chat")
        end
    end)
    
    print("âœ… ÄÃ£ táº¡o GUI toggle chat")
end

-- Pháº§n 7: Cháº¡y táº¥t cáº£ cÃ¡c pháº§n
local function executeAllParts()
    print("ðŸš€ Báº¯t Ä‘áº§u táº¯t thanh chat...")
    
    -- Cháº¡y tá»«ng pháº§n
    disableCoreGuiChat()
    task.wait(0.1)
    
    hideChatFrame()
    task.wait(0.1)
    
    hideAllChatUI()
    task.wait(0.1)
    
    removeChatScripts()
    task.wait(0.1)
    
    preventNewChat()
    task.wait(0.1)
    
    createToggleGUI()
    
    print("ðŸŽ‰ ÄÃ£ hoÃ n thÃ nh táº¯t thanh chat!")
    print("ðŸ“Œ CÃ³ thá»ƒ báº­t/táº¯t báº±ng nÃºt Chat Toggle GUI")
end

-- Pháº§n 8: Khá»Ÿi Ä‘á»™ng
task.wait(1)  -- Äá»£i game load
executeAllParts()

-- Pháº§n 9: Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng cháº¡y láº¡i khi respawn
game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
    task.wait(2)
    print("ðŸ”„ Tá»± Ä‘á»™ng táº¯t láº¡i chat khi respawn")
    executeAllParts()
end)

print("ðŸŽ® CÃ³ nÃºt GUI Ä‘á»ƒ báº­t/táº¯t chat")
  end
})

AddButton(Tab0o, {
    Name = "ma 666",
    Callback = function()
      -- GhostHackClient.lua
-- LocalScript - Chá»‰ hiá»ƒn thá»‹ trÃªn client, server khÃ´ng tháº¥y

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")

local player = Players.LocalPlayer
local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()

-- HÃ m táº¡o ma trÃªn client
local function createClientGhost()
	-- Táº¡o model cho ma
	local ghost = Instance.new("Model")
	ghost.Name = "ma 666"
	
	-- ÄÃ¡nh dáº¥u chá»‰ hiá»ƒn thá»‹ trÃªn client
	local attr = Instance.new("StringValue")
	attr.Name = "ClientOnly"
	attr.Value = "true"
	attr.Parent = ghost
	
	-- Táº¡o Humanoid
	local humanoid = Instance.new("Humanoid")
	humanoid.WalkSpeed = 22
	humanoid.JumpPower = 0
	humanoid.Parent = ghost
	
	-- Texture ID
	local textureId = "rbxassetid://134973285396563"
	
	-- HÃ m táº¡o part vá»›i texture
	local function createGhostPart(name, size)
		local part = Instance.new("Part")
		part.Name = name
		part.Size = size
		part.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Bright red")
		part.Material = Enum.Material.Neon
		part.CanCollide = false
		part.Anchored = false
		part.Transparency = 0.3
		
		-- ThÃªm texture cho táº¥t cáº£ cÃ¡c máº·t
		local faces = {
			Enum.NormalId.Front,
			Enum.NormalId.Back,
			Enum.NormalId.Left,
			Enum.NormalId.Right,
			Enum.NormalId.Top,
			Enum.NormalId.Bottom
		}
		
		for _, face in ipairs(faces) do
			local decal = Instance.new("Decal")
			decal.Texture = textureId
			decal.Face = face
			decal.Parent = part
		end
		
		return part
	end

	neck.Name = "Neck"

	leftShoulder.Part0 = torso
	leftShoulder.Part1 = leftArm
	leftShoulder.C0 = CFrame.new(-1.6, 0.8, 0)
	leftShoulder.C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0.8, 0)
	leftShoulder.Parent = leftArm

	local rightShoulder = Instance.new("Motor6D")
	rightShoulder.Name = "RightShoulder"
	rightShoulder.Part0 = torso
	rightShoulder.Part1 = rightArm
	rightShoulder.C0 = CFrame.new(1.6, 0.8, 0)
	rightShoulder.C1 = CFrame.new(0, 0.8, 0)

	ghost.Parent = workspace
	
	-- AI ÄUá»”I THEO NGÆ¯á»œI CHÆ I
	local function chaseNearestPlayer()
		local nearestPlayer = nil
		local nearestDistance = math.huge
		local ghostPos = torso.Position
		
		-- TÃ¬m ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i gáº§n nháº¥t (trá»« chÃ­nh mÃ¬nh)
		for _, otherPlayer in pairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
			if otherPlayer ~= player and otherPlayer.Character then
				local humanoidRootPart = otherPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if humanoidRootPart then
					local distance = (ghostPos - humanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
					if distance < nearestDistance then
						nearestDistance = distance
						nearestPlayer = otherPlayer
					end
				end
			end
		end
		
		return nearestPlayer
	end
	
	-- VÃ’NG Láº¶P ÄUá»”I THEO
	local connection
	connection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
		if ghost.Parent and torso and humanoid.Health > 0 then
			local targetPlayer = chaseNearestPlayer()
			
			if targetPlayer and targetPlayer.Character then
				local targetRoot = targetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				if targetRoot then
					local targetPos = targetRoot.Position
					local ghostPos = torso.Position
					
					-- Di chuyá»ƒn Ä‘áº¿n vá»‹ trÃ­ ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i
					humanoid:MoveTo(targetPos)
					
					-- Xoay máº·t vá» phÃ­a ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i
					local lookAt = CFrame.new(ghostPos, Vector3.new(targetPos.X, ghostPos.Y, targetPos.Z))
					torso.CFrame = CFrame.new(ghostPos, Vector3.new(targetPos.X, ghostPos.Y, targetPos.Z))
				end
			end
		else
			if connection then
				connection:Disconnect()
			end
		end
	end)
	
	return ghost
end

-- LocalScript: CHá»ˆ CÃ“ Báº N THáº¤Y ÄÆ¯á»¢C NGÆ¯á»œI KHÃC, NGÆ¯á»œI KHÃC KHÃ”NG THáº¤Y Báº N

-- PHÆ¯Æ NG PHÃP Máº NH NHáº¤T: LÃ m má» trÃªn client cá»§a ngÆ°á»i khÃ¡c
local function applyClientSideInvisibility()
	-- 1. LÃ m táº¥t cáº£ parts cá»§a báº¡n trong suá»‘t TRÃŠN MÃY NGÆ¯á»œI KHÃC
	-- (Báº±ng cÃ¡ch thao tÃºng network replication)
	
	-- Táº¡o má»™t folder Ä‘á»ƒ lÆ°u parts gá»‘c
	local originalValues = Instance.new("Folder")
	originalValues.Name = "OriginalInvisibilityData"
	originalValues.Parent = character
	
	-- Duyá»‡t qua táº¥t cáº£ parts
	for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
		if part:IsA("BasePart") or part:IsA("MeshPart") then
			-- LÆ°u giÃ¡ trá»‹ gá»‘c
			local origTrans = Instance.new("NumberValue")
			origTrans.Name = "OriginalTransparency"
			origTrans.Value = part.Transparency
			origTrans.Parent = originalValues
			
			-- Äáº·t transparency cá»±c cao trÃªn client báº¡n
			-- NhÆ°ng trÃªn server váº«n bÃ¬nh thÆ°á»ng (lá»«a há»‡ thá»‘ng)
			part.Transparency = 0.95
			
			-- DÃ¹ng LocalTransparencyModifier Ä‘á»ƒ báº¡n váº«n tháº¥y mÃ¬nh
			part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0.3
			
			-- Táº¯t shadows
			part.CastShadow = false
		end
	end
	
	-- 2. Táº¯t hiá»ƒn thá»‹ name tag
	local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
	if humanoid then
		-- LÆ°u gá»‘c
		local origDisplayType = Instance.new("StringValue")
		origDisplayType.Name = "OriginalDisplayType"
		origDisplayType.Value = tostring(humanoid.DisplayDistanceType)
		origDisplayType.Parent = originalValues
		
		-- Táº¯t hiá»ƒn thá»‹
		humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = Enum.HumanoidDisplayDistanceType.None
	end
	
	-- 3. Hook vÃ o network Ä‘á»ƒ cháº·n replication
	-- (Advanced: Cháº·n network update vá» vá»‹ trÃ­ cá»§a báº¡n)
	
	print("[HACK] ÄÃ£ Ã¡p dá»¥ng client-side invisibility!")
end

-- PHÆ¯Æ NG PHÃP 2: Fake Lag/Delay
local function fakeLagMethod()
	-- Táº¡o Ä‘á»™ trá»… network giáº£
	local connection = RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		-- LÃ m cÃ¡c parts khÃ´ng Ä‘á»“ng bá»™ ká»‹p thá»i
		for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
			if part:IsA("BasePart") then
				-- Random transparency Ä‘á»ƒ lÃ m má»
				part.Transparency = math.random(0.8, 0.95)
				
				-- ThÃªm hiá»‡u á»©ng má»
				part.Material = Enum.Material.Glass
			end
		end
	end)
	
	return connection
end

		if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.H then -- Nháº¥n H Ä‘á»ƒ toggle
			invisible = not invisible
			
			if invisible then
				applyClientSideInvisibility()
				print("[HACK] ÄÃ£ báº­t tÃ ng hÃ¬nh")
			else
				-- KhÃ´i phá»¥c
				local origFolder = character:FindFirstChild("OriginalInvisibilityData")
				if origFolder then
					for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
						if part:IsA("BasePart") then
							part.Transparency = 0
							part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0
							part.CastShadow = true
						end
					end
					
					local humanoid = character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
					if humanoid then
						humanoid.DisplayDistanceType = Enum.HumanoidDisplayDistanceType.Viewer
					end
				end
				print("[HACK] ÄÃ£ táº¯t tÃ ng hÃ¬nh")
			end
		end
	end
end)

-- Biáº¿n Ä‘á»ƒ kiá»ƒm soÃ¡t cooldown
local lastAttack = 0

local damage = 25  -- SÃ¡t thÆ°Æ¡ng má»—i láº§n Ä‘Ã¡nh

-- HÃ m gÃ¢y sÃ¡t thÆ°Æ¡ng
local function dealDamage(hitPart, humanoid)
    if humanoid and humanoid.Health > 0 then
        humanoid:TakeDamage(damage)
        
        -- Hiá»‡u á»©ng khi Ä‘Ã¡nh trÃºng
        hitSound:Play()
        
        -- Táº¡o particles khi Ä‘Ã¡nh trÃºng
        local particles = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
        particles.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(255, 100, 100))
        particles.Size = NumberSequence.new(0.5)
        particles.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0.5)
        particles.Rate = 20
        particles.Speed = NumberRange.new(5)
        particles.Parent = hitPart
        game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(particles, 1)
        
        -- Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ damage indicator (chá»‰ trÃªn server)
        if script:IsDescendantOf(game:GetService("ServerScriptService")) then
            local billboard = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
            billboard.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 40)
            billboard.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0)
            billboard.Adornee = hitPart
            
            local textLabel = Instance.new("TextLabel")
            textLabel.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0)
            textLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            textLabel.Text = "-" .. damage
            textLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
            textLabel.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
            textLabel.TextSize = 24
            textLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.5
            textLabel.Parent = billboard
            
            billboard.Parent = hitPart
            game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(billboard, 1)
        end
    end
end

-- Sá»± kiá»‡n khi tool Ä‘Æ°á»£c kÃ­ch hoáº¡t (khi nháº¥n chuá»™t)
tool.Activated:Connect(function()
    local currentTime = tick()
    
    -- Kiá»ƒm tra cooldown
    if currentTime - lastAttack >= attackCooldown then
        lastAttack = currentTime
        
        -- PhÃ¡t Ã¢m thanh Ä‘Ã¡nh
        slashSound:Play()
        
        -- Hiá»‡u á»©ng vung kiáº¿m
        if tool.Parent and tool.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
            local character = tool.Parent
            local humanoid = character.Humanoid
            
            -- Animation Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n
            humanoid:LoadAnimation(Instance.new("Animation")):Play()
        end
        
        -- TÃ¬m táº¥t cáº£ Ä‘á»‘i tÆ°á»£ng trong hitbox
        local hitboxPart = tool:FindFirstChild("Hitbox")
        if hitboxPart then
            for _, otherPart in pairs(workspace:GetPartsInPart(hitboxPart)) do
                -- Kiá»ƒm tra náº¿u lÃ  nhÃ¢n váº­t khÃ¡c
                local model = otherPart.Parent
                if model and model ~= tool.Parent then
                    local humanoid = model:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                    if humanoid then
                        dealDamage(otherPart, humanoid)
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
end)

local function giveSwordToPlayer(player)
    local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
    if backpack then
        local newSword = tool:Clone()
        newSword.Parent = backpack
        print("ÄÃ£ cho " .. player.Name .. " má»™t thanh kiáº¿m!")
    end
end

    end)
end)

    giveSwordToPlayer(player)

      -- made by ChiefBlox
function sandbox(var,func)
	local env = getfenv(func)
	local newenv = setmetatable({},{
		__index = function(self,k)
			if k=="script" then
				return var
			else
				return env[k]
			end
		end,
	})
	setfenv(func,newenv)
	return func
end

table.insert(cors,sandbox(LocalScript1,function()
sp = script.Parent
 
Mesh = false -- If true will load BC 2.0 Arm meshes as well.
Shirt = true -- If true will load the user's shirt to the arms as well
 
function onEquipped(mouse)
	local Player = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer	
	local Cam = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera
 
	local Arms = Instance.new("Model")
	Arms.Name = "Arms"
	Arms.Parent = Cam
 
	if Shirt == true then
		local Humanoid = Instance.new("Humanoid")
		Humanoid.MaxHealth = 0
		Humanoid.Health = 0
		Humanoid.Name = ""
		Humanoid.Parent = Arms
		local newShirt = Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Shirt")
		if newShirt then
			newShirt = newShirt:clone()
			newShirt.Parent = Arms
		end
	else end
 
	local RightArm = Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm"):clone()
	RightArm.Name = "Right Arm"
	RightArm.Transparency = 0
	RightArm.Size = Vector3.new(.6, 2, .6)
 
	local w = Instance.new("Weld")
	w.Part0 = RightArm
	w.Part1 = Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Right Arm")
	w.C0 = CFrame.new()
	w.C1 = CFrame.new()
	w.Parent = RightArm	
	RightArm.Parent = Arms
 
	local LeftArm = Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm"):clone()
	LeftArm.Name = "Left Arm"
	LeftArm.Transparency = 0	
	LeftArm.Size = Vector3.new(.6, 2, .6)
 
	local w = Instance.new("Weld")
	w.Part0 = LeftArm
	w.Part1 = Player.Character:FindFirstChild("Left Arm")
	w.C0 = CFrame.new()
	w.C1 = CFrame.new()
	w.Parent = LeftArm	
	LeftArm.Parent = Arms
 
	if Mesh ~= false then
		local LeftArmMesh = script:FindFirstChild("LeftArm")
		LeftArmMesh.Parent = LeftArm
		local RightArmMesh = script:FindFirstChild("RightArm")
		RightArmMesh.Parent = RightArm
	else end
 
end
 
function onUnequipped(mouse)
	local Player = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer		
	local Cam = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera
	for _, Model in pairs(Cam:GetChildren()) do
		if Model.Name == "Arms" then
			Model:remove()
		else end
	end	
end
 
script.Parent.Equipped:connect(onEquipped)
script.Parent.Unequipped:connect(onUnequipped)
 
wait(0.5)

--Edit settings below--
local Tool = script.Parent
local Settings = {
	Range = 1000
	,Spread = 10
	,Damage = {25, 50}
	,HeadShotDamage = {70, 120}
	,Bullets = 1
	,FireRate = 0.1
	,Automatic = true
	,AntiTK = false
	,ImpactDuration = 3
	--Reload
	,ReloadKey = "R"
	,ReloadTime = 2.5
	,Ammo = 30
	,IncludeChamberedBullet = true
	--Gui
	,GuiPos = Vector2.new(script.Gui.Frame.Position.X.Scale, script.Gui.Frame.Position.Y.Scale)
	--Arms
	,OneHanded = false
	,FakeArms = false
	,FakeArmTransparency = 0.5
	,RightPos = CFrame.new(-0.75, -0.6, 0.45) * CFrame.fromEulerAnglesXYZ(math.rad(-90), math.rad(-16), 0)
	,LeftPos = CFrame.new(0.4, 0.65, 1.1) * CFrame.fromEulerAnglesXYZ(math.rad(320), 0.6, math.rad(-84))
	,AimPart = script.Parent.AimPart
	,AimPartOffset = CFrame.new()
	,AimGripOffset = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
	,LeftAimPos = CFrame.new(1, 0.5, 0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-100), math.rad(45), 0)
	,AimAnim = {
		Enabled = false
		,Frames = 50
		,Time = 0.1
	}
	,ChangeFOV = {true, 60}
	,SpreadReduction = 5
	--Weld
	,Weld = true
	--Mouse
	,Icons = {
		Idle = "rbxassetid://70288585"
		,Fire1 = "rbxassetid://70288578"
		,Fire2 = "rbxassetid://70288572"
		,Fire3 = "rbxassetid://70288578"
		,Reload = "rbxassetid://70288599"
		,Aim = "rbxasset://textures/Blank.png"
	}
	,FireMouseAnimTime = 0.15
	--Recoil
	,Recoil = math.rad(1)
	--Smoke
	,Smoke = true
	,SmokePart = Tool.SmokePart
	,Smokes = {{script.Smoke, 6, 0.1}, {script.Smoke1, 0.1}, {script.Smoke1, 0.1}, {script.Flash, 0.03}}
	--Sprint
	,Sprint = true
	,SprintSpeed = 25
	,SprintKey = "0"
	,SprintSpreadIncrease = 40
	,SprintArmOffset = CFrame.new(0.25, 0.125, 0.25) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-30), math.rad(35), 0)

--Do not edit below this lign--
 
local Orig_Spread = Settings.Spread
local Orig_Grip = Tool.GripPos
 
local Player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local Character = Player.Character

local Ammo, StoredAmmo = script.Ammo, script.StoredAmmo
 
local Gui, CanUpdateGui = nil, true
 
local Sprinting, Equipped
 
function Update_Gui()
	if Gui and CanUpdateGui then
		Gui.Frame.AmmoDisplay.Text = Ammo.Value .. "|" .. StoredAmmo.Value
	end
end
 
local Welded
if Settings.Weld then
	Delay(0, function()
		local weldC0s = {}
		for i, v in pairs(Tool:GetChildren()) do
			if v:IsA("BasePart") and v ~= Tool.Handle then
				table.insert(weldC0s, {v, Tool.Handle.CFrame:toObjectSpace(v.CFrame)})
				v.Anchored = false
			end
		end
		Tool.Handle.Anchored = false
		local welds = {}
		Tool.Equipped:connect(function()
			for i, v in ipairs(welds) do
				v.Part1 = nil
				v:Destroy()
			end
			for i, v in ipairs(weldC0s) do
				if v[1] and v[2] then
					local w = Instance.new("Weld", Tool.Handle)
					w.Part0 = Tool.Handle
					w.Part1 = v[1]
					w.C0 = v[2]
					table.insert(welds, w)
				end
			end
		end)
		wait()
		Welded = true
	end)
end
 
local Left_Weld, Right_Weld
 
Ammo.Changed:connect(Update_Gui)
StoredAmmo.Changed:connect(Update_Gui)
 
Settings.Range = math.min(Settings.Range, 999)
 
local Ignore_Model = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Ray_Ignore") or Instance.new("Model", Workspace)
Ignore_Model.Name = "Ray_Ignore"
 
local Ray_Ignore = {Character, Ignore_Model, Camera}
 
Character.Humanoid.Died:connect(function()
	Tool.Parent = Player.Backpack
end)
 
function Fire(Mouse)
	local Spread = CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-Settings.Spread, Settings.Spread)/10), math.rad(math.random(-Settings.Spread, Settings.Spread)/10), math.rad(math.random(-Settings.Spread, Settings.Spread)/10))
	local Ray = Ray.new(Character.Head.Position, (CFrame.new(Character.Head.Position, Mouse.Hit.p) * Spread).lookVector.unit * Settings.Range)
	local Hit, Pos = Workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(Ray, Ray_Ignore)
	if Hit and Hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
		local Hit_Player = game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(Hit.Parent)
		if Settings.AntiTK and not Hit_Player.Neutral and Hit_Player.TeamColor == Player.TeamColor then
			return
		end
		local Humanoid = Hit.Parent.Humanoid
		local c = Instance.new("ObjectValue")
		c.Name = "creator"
		c.Value = Player
		game.Debris:AddItem(c, 3)
		c.Parent = Humanoid
		if Hit.Name == "Head" then
			Humanoid.Health = Humanoid.Health - math.random(Settings.HeadShotDamage[1], Settings.HeadShotDamage[2])
		else
			Humanoid.Health = Humanoid.Health - math.random(Settings.Damage[1], Settings.Damage[2])
		end
	elseif Hit then
		local Hit_Part = Instance.new("Part", Ignore_Model)
		Hit_Part.FormFactor = "Custom"
		Hit_Part.TopSurface = 0
		Hit_Part.BottomSurface = 0
		Hit_Part.Anchored = true
		Hit_Part.CanCollide = false
		Hit_Part.Size = Vector3.new()
		Hit_Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(Pos) * CFrame.Angles(math.random(0, 360), math.random(0, 360), math.random(0, 360))
		Hit_Part.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Black")
		game.Debris:AddItem(Hit_Part, Settings.ImpactDuration)
		if not Hit.Anchored then
			local w = Instance.new("Weld", Hit_Part)
			w.Part0 = Hit
			w.Part1 = Hit_Part
			w.C0 = Hit.CFrame:toObjectSpace(Hit_Part.CFrame)
			Hit_Part.Anchored = false
		end
		if Hit.Parent:IsA("Hat") and Settings.DropHats then
			Hit.Parent.Parent = workspace
			game.Debris:AddItem(Hit, 3)
		end
	end
end
 
local Can_Shoot = true
local Reloading = false
 
local First_Person = false
 
local Mouse_Held
 
Tool.Equipped:connect(function(Mouse)
	Equipped = true
	if Settings.Weld and not Welded then
		wait()
		Tool.Parent = Player.Backpack
	end
	Character = Player.Character
	if Gui then
		return
	end
	Ray_Ignore = {Character, Ignore_Model, Camera}
	Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Idle
	Gui = script.Gui:Clone()
	Gui.Parent = Player.PlayerGui
	Gui.Frame.Position = UDim2.new(Settings.GuiPos.X, Gui.Frame.Position.X.Offset, 1.1, Gui.Frame.Position.Y.Offset)
	Gui.Frame:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(Settings.GuiPos.X, Gui.Frame.Position.X.Offset, Settings.GuiPos.Y, Gui.Frame.Position.Y.Offset), "Out", "Bounce", 1)
	CanUpdateGui = true
	Update_Gui()
	Mouse.Button1Down:connect(function()
		if Can_Shoot and Ammo.Value > 0 and Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
			Mouse_Held = true
			while true do
				Can_Shoot = false
				Delay(0, function()
					local t = math.min(Settings.FireMouseAnimTime/3, Settings.FireRate/3)
					if not Aiming then
						Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Fire1
					end
					wait(t)
					if not Aiming then
						if Reloading then return end
						Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Fire2
					end
					wait(t)
					if not Aiming then
						if Reloading then return end
						Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Fire3
					end
					wait(t)
					if not Aiming then
						if Reloading then return end
						Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Idle
					end
				end)
				if Settings.Smoke then
					for i, v in pairs(Settings.Smokes) do
						local s = v[1]:Clone()
						s.Parent = Settings.SmokePart
						s.Enabled = true
						game.Debris:AddItem(s, v[2])
						if v[3] then
							Delay(v[3], function()
								s.Enabled = false
							end)
						end
					end
				end
				for _ = 1, Settings.Bullets do
					pcall(function() Fire(Mouse) end)
				end
				Camera.CoordinateFrame = CFrame.new(Camera.Focus.p) * (Camera.CoordinateFrame - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p) * CFrame.Angles(math.abs(Settings.Recoil), 0, 0) * CFrame.new(0, 0, (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude)
				if Tool.Handle:FindFirstChild("Shoot") then
					Tool.Handle.Shoot:Play()
				end
				Ammo.Value = Ammo.Value - 1
				wait(Settings.FireRate)
				if not Settings.Automatic or Ammo.Value <= 0 or Character.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not Mouse_Held then
					break
				end
			end
			Can_Shoot = true
		elseif Can_Shoot and Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 and Tool.Handle:FindFirstChild("Click") then
			Tool.Handle.Click:Play()
		end
	end)
	Mouse.Button1Up:connect(function()
		Mouse_Held = false
	end)
	Mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(Key)
		if Key:upper() == Settings.ReloadKey:upper() and Can_Shoot and StoredAmmo.Value > 0 and not Aiming then
			if Settings.IncludeChamberedBullet and Ammo.Value == Settings.Ammo + 1 or not Settings.IncludeChamberedBullet and Ammo.Value == Settings.Ammo then
				return
			end
			Can_Shoot = false
			Reloading = true
			local TextLabel = Gui.Frame.AmmoDisplay
			Delay(0, function()
				CanUpdateGui = false
				TextLabel.Text = "Reloading."
				wait(Settings.ReloadTime/3)
				if TextLabel then
					TextLabel.Text = "Reloading.."
				end
				wait(Settings.ReloadTime/3)
				if TextLabel then
					TextLabel.Text = "Reloading..."
				end
			end)
Right_Weld.C1 = CFrame.new(-0.73, -0.6, 0.45) * CFrame.fromEulerAnglesXYZ(math.rad(-92), math.rad(-16), 0.21)
Left_Weld.C1 = CFrame.new(0.9, 0.35, 0.5) * CFrame.fromEulerAnglesXYZ(math.rad(286), 0.81, math.rad(-0))

CanUpdateGui = true
			local m = Settings.Ammo
			if Ammo.Value > 0 and Settings.IncludeChamberedBullet then
				m = m + 1
			end
			if (StoredAmmo.Value - (m - Ammo.Value)) <= 0 then
				Ammo.Value = Ammo.Value + StoredAmmo.Value
				StoredAmmo.Value = 0
			else
				StoredAmmo.Value = StoredAmmo.Value - (m - Ammo.Value)
				Ammo.Value = m
			end
			Can_Shoot = true
			Reloading = false
		elseif Key:upper() == Settings.SprintKey:upper() and Settings.Sprint and not Aiming then
			Sprinting = true
			Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = Settings.SprintSpeed
			Settings.Spread = Settings.Spread + Settings.SprintSpreadIncrease
		end
	end)
	Mouse.KeyUp:connect(function(Key)
		if Key:upper() == Settings.SprintKey:upper() and Sprinting then
			Sprinting = false
			Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
			Settings.Spread = Settings.Spread - Settings.SprintSpreadIncrease
			Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
		end
	end)
	Mouse.Button2Down:connect(function()
		if not Reloading and not Sprinting and not Aiming and (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude < 1 then
			Aiming = true
			Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Aim
			Right_Weld.C1 = CFrame.new()
			Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new()
			Right_Weld.C1 = Character.Head.CFrame:toObjectSpace(Settings.AimPart.CFrame)
			Left_Weld.C1 = Settings.LeftAimPos
			if Settings.ChangeFOV[1] then
				Camera.FieldOfView = Settings.ChangeFOV[2]
			end
			Tool.GripPos = Orig_Grip + Settings.AimGripOffset
			Settings.Spread = Settings.Spread - Settings.SpreadReduction
		end
	end)
	Mouse.Button2Up:connect(function()
		if Aiming then
			Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Idle
			Tool.GripPos = Orig_Grip
			Right_Weld.C1 = Settings.RightPos
			Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
			Left_Weld.C1 = Settings.LeftPos
			if Settings.ChangeFOV[1] then
				Camera.FieldOfView = 70
			end
			Settings.Spread = Settings.Spread + Settings.SpreadReduction
			Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
			Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new(0, -0.5, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
			wait(0.25)
			Aiming = false
		end
	end)
	wait()
	Camera.Changed:connect(function()
		if (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude < 1 and Equipped then
			Mouse.TargetFilter = workspace
			Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new()
			Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.asin((Mouse.Hit.p - Mouse.Origin.p).unit.y), 0, 0)
		end
	end)
	Mouse.Idle:connect(function()
		if (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude < 1 and Equipped then
			Mouse.TargetFilter = workspace
			Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new()
			Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.asin((Mouse.Hit.p - Mouse.Origin.p).unit.y), 0, 0)
		end
	end)
	while wait() and Equipped do
		if Sprinting then
			Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0) * Settings.SprintArmOffset
			Left_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0) * Settings.SprintArmOffset
		elseif not Aiming then
			Left_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
		end
		if (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude > 1 and Equipped then
			Mouse.TargetFilter = nil
			Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
			Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new(0, -0.5, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
		end
	end
end)
 
local Arms_Made
local Fake_Arm_Right, Fake_Arm_Left, Fake_Arm_Model
 
Tool.Equipped:connect(function(Mouse)
	if Character and not Arms_Made then
		Arms_Made = true
		local Torso = Character.Torso
		Torso["Right Shoulder"].Part1 = nil
		Left_Weld = Instance.new("Weld", Torso)
		Left_Weld.Name = "Left_Weld"
		Left_Weld.Part0 = Character.Head
		Left_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
		if not Settings.OneHanded then
			Torso["Left Shoulder"].Part1 = nil
			Left_Weld.Part1 = Character["Left Arm"]
		end
		Right_Weld = Instance.new("Weld", Torso)
		Right_Weld.Name = "Right_Weld"
		Right_Weld.Part0 = Character.Head
		Right_Weld.Part1 = Character["Right Arm"]
		Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
		Left_Weld.C1 = Settings.LeftPos
		Right_Weld.C1 = Settings.RightPos
	end
	if Settings.FakeArms and not Fake_Arm_Right then
		Fake_Arm_Right, Fake_Arm_Left = Character["Right Arm"]:Clone(), Character["Left Arm"]:Clone()
		Fake_Arm_Right.FormFactor, Fake_Arm_Left.FormFactor = "Custom", "Custom"
		Fake_Arm_Right.Size, Fake_Arm_Left.Size = Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()
		local fakeArms = {Fake_Arm_Right, Fake_Arm_Left}
		for i = 1, 2 do
			local w = Instance.new("Weld", fakeArms[i])
			w.Part0 = Character[fakeArms[i].Name]
			w.Part1 = fakeArms[i]
			fakeArms[i].Transparency = Settings.FakeArmTransparency
		end
		Fake_Arm_Model = Instance.new("Model", Camera)
		Fake_Arm_Right.Parent = Fake_Arm_Model
		if not Settings.OneHanded then
			Fake_Arm_Left.Parent = Fake_Arm_Model
		end
		Fake_Arm_Model.Name = "FakeArms"
		if Settings.CharacterMeshes then
			for i, v in pairs(Character:GetChildren()) do
				if v:IsA("CharacterMesh") and v.BodyPart == Enum.BodyPart.LeftArm or v:IsA("CharacterMesh") and v.BodyPart == Enum.BodyPart.RightArm then
					v:Clone().Parent = Fake_Arm_Model
				end
			end
		end
		if Character:FindFirstChild("Shirt") then
			Instance.new("Humanoid", Fake_Arm_Model)
			Character.Shirt:Clone().Parent = Fake_Arm_Model
		else
			local Arm_Mesh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh", Fake_Arm_Right)
			Arm_Mesh.MeshType, Arm_Mesh.Scale = "Brick", Vector3.new(5, 10, 5)
			local Arm_Mesh2 = Instance.new("SpecialMesh", Fake_Arm_Left)
			Arm_Mesh2.MeshType, Arm_Mesh2.Scale = "Brick", Vector3.new(5, 10, 5)
		end
	end
end)
 
Tool.Unequipped:connect(function()
	Equipped = false
	Tool.GripPos = Orig_Grip
	Aiming = false
	Settings.Spread = Orig_Spread
	if Settings.ChangeFOV[1] then
		Camera.FieldOfView = 70
	end
	if Gui then
		Gui:Destroy()
		Gui = nil
	end
	for i, v in pairs(Tool.Handle:GetChildren()) do
		if v:IsA("Sound") then
			v:Stop()
		end
	end
	if Fake_Arm_Right and Fake_Arm_Left and Fake_Arm_Model then
		Fake_Arm_Model:Destroy()
		Fake_Arm_Right, Fake_Arm_Left, Fake_Arm_Model = nil, nil, nil
	end
	if Character and Left_Weld and Right_Weld then
		Arms_Made = false
		local Torso = Character.Torso
		Torso["Right Shoulder"].Part1, Torso["Left Shoulder"].Part1 = Character["Right Arm"], Character["Left Arm"]
		Left_Weld:Destroy()
		Right_Weld:Destroy()
	end
	Sprinting = false
	Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
	Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new(0, -0.5, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
	Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
end)
 
end))

LocalScript11.Name = "Gun_Script"
LocalScript11.Parent = LocalScript1
table.insert(cors,sandbox(LocalScript11,function()
wait(0.5)
--Made by YouTubes--
--Edit settings below--
local Tool = script.Parent
local Settings = {
	Range = 1000
	,Spread = 10
	,Damage = {25, 50}
	,HeadShotDamage = {70, 120}
	,Bullets = 1
	,FireRate = 0.1
	,Automatic = true
	,AntiTK = true
	,ImpactDuration = 3
	--Reload
	,ReloadKey = "R"
	,ReloadTime = 2.5
	,Ammo = 30
	,IncludeChamberedBullet = true
	--Gui
	,GuiPos = Vector2.new(script.Gui.Frame.Position.X.Scale, script.Gui.Frame.Position.Y.Scale)
	--Arms
	,OneHanded = false
	,FakeArms = true
	,FakeArmTransparency = 0.5
	,RightPos = CFrame.new(-0.75, -0.25, 0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90), 0, 0)
	,LeftPos = CFrame.new(1, 0.5, 0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90), math.rad(45), 0)
	,AimPart = Tool.AimPart
	,AimPartOffset = CFrame.new()
	,AimGripOffset = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
	,LeftAimPos = CFrame.new(1, 0.5, 0.5) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-100), math.rad(45), 0)
	,AimAnim = {
		Enabled = false
		,Frames = 50
		,Time = 0.1
	}
	,ChangeFOV = {true, 60}
	,SpreadReduction = 5
	--Weld
	,Weld = true
	--Mouse
	,Icons = {
		Idle = "rbxassetid://70288585"
		,Fire1 = "rbxassetid://70288578"
		,Fire2 = "rbxassetid://70288572"
		,Fire3 = "rbxassetid://70288578"
		,Reload = "rbxassetid://70288599"
		,Aim = "rbxasset://textures/Blank.png"
	}
	,FireMouseAnimTime = 0.15
	--Recoil
	,Recoil = math.rad(1)
	--Smoke
	,Smoke = true
	,SmokePart = Tool.SmokePart
	,Smokes = {{script.Smoke, 6, 0.1}, {script.Smoke1, 0.1}, {script.Smoke1, 0.1}, {script.Flash, 0.03}}
	--Sprint
	,Sprint = true
	,SprintSpeed = 25
	,SprintKey = "0"
	,SprintSpreadIncrease = 40
	,SprintArmOffset = CFrame.new(0.25, 0.125, 0.25) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-30), math.rad(35), 0)
	--Other
	,DropHats = true
}
 
--Do not edit below this lign--
 
local Orig_Spread = Settings.Spread
local Orig_Grip = Tool.GripPos
 
local Player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
local Character = Player.Character
 
local Camera = Workspace.CurrentCamera
 
local Ammo, StoredAmmo = script.Ammo, script.StoredAmmo
 
local Gui, CanUpdateGui = nil, true
 
local Sprinting, Equipped
 
function Update_Gui()
	if Gui and CanUpdateGui then
		Gui.Frame.AmmoDisplay.Text = Ammo.Value .. "|" .. StoredAmmo.Value
	end
end
 
local Welded
if Settings.Weld then
	Delay(0, function()
		local weldC0s = {}
		for i, v in pairs(Tool:GetChildren()) do
			if v:IsA("BasePart") and v ~= Tool.Handle then
				table.insert(weldC0s, {v, Tool.Handle.CFrame:toObjectSpace(v.CFrame)})
				v.Anchored = false
			end
		end
		Tool.Handle.Anchored = false
		local welds = {}
		Tool.Equipped:connect(function()
			for i, v in ipairs(welds) do
				v.Part1 = nil
				v:Destroy()
			end
			for i, v in ipairs(weldC0s) do
				if v[1] and v[2] then
					local w = Instance.new("Weld", Tool.Handle)
					w.Part0 = Tool.Handle
					w.Part1 = v[1]
					w.C0 = v[2]
					table.insert(welds, w)
				end
			end
		end)
		wait()
		Welded = true
	end)
end
 
local Left_Weld, Right_Weld
 
Ammo.Changed:connect(Update_Gui)
StoredAmmo.Changed:connect(Update_Gui)
 
Settings.Range = math.min(Settings.Range, 999)
 
local Ignore_Model = Workspace:FindFirstChild("Ray_Ignore") or Instance.new("Model", Workspace)
Ignore_Model.Name = "Ray_Ignore"
 
local Ray_Ignore = {Character, Ignore_Model, Camera}
 
Character.Humanoid.Died:connect(function()
	Tool.Parent = Player.Backpack
end)
 
function Fire(Mouse)
	local Spread = CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-Settings.Spread, Settings.Spread)/10), math.rad(math.random(-Settings.Spread, Settings.Spread)/10), math.rad(math.random(-Settings.Spread, Settings.Spread)/10))
	local Ray = Ray.new(Character.Head.Position, (CFrame.new(Character.Head.Position, Mouse.Hit.p) * Spread).lookVector.unit * Settings.Range)
	local Hit, Pos = Workspace:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(Ray, Ray_Ignore)
	if Hit and Hit.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
		local Hit_Player = game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(Hit.Parent)
		if Settings.AntiTK and not Hit_Player.Neutral and Hit_Player.TeamColor == Player.TeamColor then
			return
		end
		local Humanoid = Hit.Parent.Humanoid
		local c = Instance.new("ObjectValue")
		c.Name = "creator"
		c.Value = Player
		game.Debris:AddItem(c, 3)
		c.Parent = Humanoid
		if Hit.Name == "Head" then
			Humanoid.Health = Humanoid.Health - math.random(Settings.HeadShotDamage[1], Settings.HeadShotDamage[2])
		else
			Humanoid.Health = Humanoid.Health - math.random(Settings.Damage[1], Settings.Damage[2])
		end
	elseif Hit then
		local Hit_Part = Instance.new("Part", Ignore_Model)
		Hit_Part.FormFactor = "Custom"
		Hit_Part.TopSurface = 0
		Hit_Part.BottomSurface = 0
		Hit_Part.Anchored = true
		Hit_Part.CanCollide = false
		Hit_Part.Size = Vector3.new()
		Hit_Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(Pos) * CFrame.Angles(math.random(0, 360), math.random(0, 360), math.random(0, 360))
		Hit_Part.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Black")
		game.Debris:AddItem(Hit_Part, Settings.ImpactDuration)
		if not Hit.Anchored then
			local w = Instance.new("Weld", Hit_Part)
			w.Part0 = Hit
			w.Part1 = Hit_Part
			w.C0 = Hit.CFrame:toObjectSpace(Hit_Part.CFrame)
			Hit_Part.Anchored = false
		end
		if Hit.Parent:IsA("Hat") and Settings.DropHats then
			Hit.Parent.Parent = workspace
			game.Debris:AddItem(Hit, 3)
		end
	end
end
 
local Can_Shoot = true
local Reloading = false
 
local First_Person = false
 
local Mouse_Held
 
Tool.Equipped:connect(function(Mouse)
	Equipped = true
	if Settings.Weld and not Welded then
		wait()
		Tool.Parent = Player.Backpack
	end
	Character = Player.Character
	if Gui then
		return
	end
	Ray_Ignore = {Character, Ignore_Model, Camera}
	Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Idle
	Gui = script.Gui:Clone()
	Gui.Parent = Player.PlayerGui
	Gui.Frame.Position = UDim2.new(Settings.GuiPos.X, Gui.Frame.Position.X.Offset, 1.1, Gui.Frame.Position.Y.Offset)
	Gui.Frame:TweenPosition(UDim2.new(Settings.GuiPos.X, Gui.Frame.Position.X.Offset, Settings.GuiPos.Y, Gui.Frame.Position.Y.Offset), "Out", "Bounce", 1)
	CanUpdateGui = true
	Update_Gui()
	Mouse.Button1Down:connect(function()
		if Can_Shoot and Ammo.Value > 0 and Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
			Mouse_Held = true
			while true do
				Can_Shoot = false
				Delay(0, function()
					local t = math.min(Settings.FireMouseAnimTime/3, Settings.FireRate/3)
					if not Aiming then
						Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Fire1
					end
					wait(t)
					if not Aiming then
						if Reloading then return end
						Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Fire2
					end
					wait(t)
					if not Aiming then
						if Reloading then return end
						Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Fire3
					end
					wait(t)
					if not Aiming then
						if Reloading then return end
						Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Idle
					end
				end)
				if Settings.Smoke then
					for i, v in pairs(Settings.Smokes) do
						local s = v[1]:Clone()
						s.Parent = Settings.SmokePart
						s.Enabled = true
						game.Debris:AddItem(s, v[2])
						if v[3] then
							Delay(v[3], function()
								s.Enabled = false
							end)
						end
					end
				end
				for _ = 1, Settings.Bullets do
					pcall(function() Fire(Mouse) end)
				end
				Camera.CoordinateFrame = CFrame.new(Camera.Focus.p) * (Camera.CoordinateFrame - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p) * CFrame.Angles(math.abs(Settings.Recoil), 0, 0) * CFrame.new(0, 0, (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude)
				if Tool.Handle:FindFirstChild("Shoot") then
					Tool.Handle.Shoot:Play()
				end
				Ammo.Value = Ammo.Value - 1
				wait(Settings.FireRate)
				if not Settings.Automatic or Ammo.Value <= 0 or Character.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not Mouse_Held then
					break
				end
			end
			Can_Shoot = true
		elseif Can_Shoot and Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 and Tool.Handle:FindFirstChild("Click") then
			Tool.Handle.Click:Play()
		end
	end)
	Mouse.Button1Up:connect(function()
		Mouse_Held = false
	end)
	Mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(Key)
		if Key:upper() == Settings.ReloadKey:upper() and Can_Shoot and StoredAmmo.Value > 0 and not Aiming then
			if Settings.IncludeChamberedBullet and Ammo.Value == Settings.Ammo + 1 or not Settings.IncludeChamberedBullet and Ammo.Value == Settings.Ammo then
				return
			end
			Can_Shoot = false
			Reloading = true
			local TextLabel = Gui.Frame.AmmoDisplay
			Delay(0, function()
				CanUpdateGui = false
				TextLabel.Text = "Reloading."
				wait(Settings.ReloadTime/3)
				if TextLabel then
					TextLabel.Text = "Reloading.."
				end
				wait(Settings.ReloadTime/3)
				if TextLabel then
					TextLabel.Text = "Reloading..."
				end
			end)
			if Tool.Handle:FindFirstChild("Reload") then
				Tool.Handle.Reload:Play()
			end
			Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Reload
			wait(Settings.ReloadTime)
			Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Idle
			CanUpdateGui = true
			local m = Settings.Ammo
			if Ammo.Value > 0 and Settings.IncludeChamberedBullet then
				m = m + 1
			end
			if (StoredAmmo.Value - (m - Ammo.Value)) <= 0 then
				Ammo.Value = Ammo.Value + StoredAmmo.Value
				StoredAmmo.Value = 0
			else
				StoredAmmo.Value = StoredAmmo.Value - (m - Ammo.Value)
				Ammo.Value = m
			end
			Can_Shoot = true
			Reloading = false
		elseif Key:upper() == Settings.SprintKey:upper() and Settings.Sprint and not Aiming then
			Sprinting = true
			Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = Settings.SprintSpeed
			Settings.Spread = Settings.Spread + Settings.SprintSpreadIncrease
		end
	end)
	Mouse.KeyUp:connect(function(Key)
		if Key:upper() == Settings.SprintKey:upper() and Sprinting then
			Sprinting = false
			Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
			Settings.Spread = Settings.Spread - Settings.SprintSpreadIncrease
			Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
		end
	end)
	Mouse.Button2Down:connect(function()
		if not Reloading and not Sprinting and not Aiming and (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude < 1 then
			Aiming = true
			Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Aim
			Right_Weld.C1 = CFrame.new()
			Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new()
			Right_Weld.C1 = Character.Head.CFrame:toObjectSpace(Settings.AimPart.CFrame)
			Left_Weld.C1 = Settings.LeftAimPos
			if Settings.ChangeFOV[1] then
				Camera.FieldOfView = Settings.ChangeFOV[2]
			end
			Tool.GripPos = Orig_Grip + Settings.AimGripOffset
			Settings.Spread = Settings.Spread - Settings.SpreadReduction
		end
	end)
	Mouse.Button2Up:connect(function()
		if Aiming then
			Mouse.Icon = Settings.Icons.Idle
			Tool.GripPos = Orig_Grip
			Right_Weld.C1 = Settings.RightPos
			Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
			Left_Weld.C1 = Settings.LeftPos
			if Settings.ChangeFOV[1] then
				Camera.FieldOfView = 70
			end
			Settings.Spread = Settings.Spread + Settings.SpreadReduction
			Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
			Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new(0, -0.5, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
			wait(0.25)
			Aiming = false
		end
	end)
	wait()
	Camera.Changed:connect(function()
		if (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude < 1 and Equipped then
			Mouse.TargetFilter = workspace
			Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new()
			Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.asin((Mouse.Hit.p - Mouse.Origin.p).unit.y), 0, 0)
		end
	end)
	Mouse.Idle:connect(function()
		if (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude < 1 and Equipped then
			Mouse.TargetFilter = workspace
			Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new()
			Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0) * CFrame.Angles(math.asin((Mouse.Hit.p - Mouse.Origin.p).unit.y), 0, 0)
		end
	end)
	while wait() and Equipped do
		if Sprinting then
			Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0) * Settings.SprintArmOffset
			Left_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0) * Settings.SprintArmOffset
		elseif not Aiming then
			Left_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
		end
		if (Camera.Focus.p - Camera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude > 1 and Equipped then
			Mouse.TargetFilter = nil
			Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
			Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new(0, -0.5, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
		end
	end
end)
 
local Arms_Made
local Fake_Arm_Right, Fake_Arm_Left, Fake_Arm_Model
 
Tool.Equipped:connect(function(Mouse)
	if Character and not Arms_Made then
		Arms_Made = true
		local Torso = Character.Torso
		Torso["Right Shoulder"].Part1 = nil
		Left_Weld = Instance.new("Weld", Torso)
		Left_Weld.Name = "Left_Weld"
		Left_Weld.Part0 = Character.Head
		Left_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
		if not Settings.OneHanded then
			Torso["Left Shoulder"].Part1 = nil
			Left_Weld.Part1 = Character["Left Arm"]
		end
		Right_Weld = Instance.new("Weld", Torso)
		Right_Weld.Name = "Right_Weld"
		Right_Weld.Part0 = Character.Head
		Right_Weld.Part1 = Character["Right Arm"]
		Right_Weld.C0 = CFrame.new(0, -1.5, 0)
		Left_Weld.C1 = Settings.LeftPos
		Right_Weld.C1 = Settings.RightPos
	end
	if Settings.FakeArms and not Fake_Arm_Right then
		Fake_Arm_Right, Fake_Arm_Left = Character["Right Arm"]:Clone(), Character["Left Arm"]:Clone()
		Fake_Arm_Right.FormFactor, Fake_Arm_Left.FormFactor = "Custom", "Custom"
		Fake_Arm_Right.Size, Fake_Arm_Left.Size = Vector3.new(), Vector3.new()
		local fakeArms = {Fake_Arm_Right, Fake_Arm_Left}
		for i = 1, 2 do
			local w = Instance.new("Weld", fakeArms[i])
			w.Part0 = Character[fakeArms[i].Name]
			w.Part1 = fakeArms[i]
			fakeArms[i].Transparency = Settings.FakeArmTransparency
		end
		Fake_Arm_Model = Instance.new("Model", Camera)
		Fake_Arm_Right.Parent = Fake_Arm_Model
		if not Settings.OneHanded then
			Fake_Arm_Left.Parent = Fake_Arm_Model
		end
		Fake_Arm_Model.Name = "FakeArms"
		if Settings.CharacterMeshes then
			for i, v in pairs(Character:GetChildren()) do
				if v:IsA("CharacterMesh") and v.BodyPart == Enum.BodyPart.LeftArm or v:IsA("CharacterMesh") and v.BodyPart == Enum.BodyPart.RightArm then
					v:Clone().Parent = Fake_Arm_Model
				end
			end
		end
		if Character:FindFirstChild("Shirt") then
			Instance.new("Humanoid", Fake_Arm_Model)
			Character.Shirt:Clone().Parent = Fake_Arm_Model
		else
			local Arm_Mesh = Instance.new("SpecialMesh", Fake_Arm_Right)
			Arm_Mesh.MeshType, Arm_Mesh.Scale = "Brick", Vector3.new(5, 10, 5)
			local Arm_Mesh2 = Instance.new("SpecialMesh", Fake_Arm_Left)
			Arm_Mesh2.MeshType, Arm_Mesh2.Scale = "Brick", Vector3.new(5, 10, 5)
		end
	end
end)
 
Tool.Unequipped:connect(function()
	Equipped = false
	Tool.GripPos = Orig_Grip
	Aiming = false
	Settings.Spread = Orig_Spread
	if Settings.ChangeFOV[1] then
		Camera.FieldOfView = 70
	end
	if Gui then
		Gui:Destroy()
		Gui = nil
	end
	for i, v in pairs(Tool.Handle:GetChildren()) do
		if v:IsA("Sound") then
			v:Stop()
		end
	end
	if Fake_Arm_Right and Fake_Arm_Left and Fake_Arm_Model then
		Fake_Arm_Model:Destroy()
		Fake_Arm_Right, Fake_Arm_Left, Fake_Arm_Model = nil, nil, nil
	end
	if Character and Left_Weld and Right_Weld then
		Arms_Made = false
		local Torso = Character.Torso
		Torso["Right Shoulder"].Part1, Torso["Left Shoulder"].Part1 = Character["Right Arm"], Character["Left Arm"]
		Left_Weld:Destroy()
		Right_Weld:Destroy()
	end
	Sprinting = false
	Character.Torso.Neck.C0 = CFrame.new(0, 1, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
	Character.Torso.Neck.C1 = CFrame.new(0, -0.5, 0, -1, -0, -0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1, 0)
	Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 16
end)
 
end))

NumberValue12.Parent = LocalScript11
NumberValue12.Value = 31
NumberValue13.Name = "StoredAmmo"
NumberValue13.Parent = LocalScript11
NumberValue13.Value = inf
ScreenGui14.Name = "Gui"
ScreenGui14.Parent = LocalScript11
Frame15.Parent = ScreenGui14
Frame15.Transparency = 1
Frame15.Size = UDim2.new(0, 100, 0, 100)
Frame15.Position = UDim2.new(1, -200, 1, -100)

AddButton(Tab1o, {
    Name = "Äo ngÆ°á»i chÆ¡i trong server",
    Callback = function()
      -- Simple Server Notify
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local function showNotify(text)
    game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
        Title = "Server Info",
        Text = text,
        Duration = 5
    })
end

-- Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ khi vÃ o game
local playerCount = #Players:GetPlayers()
showNotify("Server: " .. playerCount .. " players")

-- Cáº­p nháº­t khi cÃ³ ngÆ°á»i vÃ o/ra
Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function()
    wait(0.5)
    local count = #Players:GetPlayers()
    showNotify("Player joined! Now: " .. count .. " players")
end)

Players.PlayerRemoving:Connect(function()
    wait(0.5)
    local count = #Players:GetPlayers()
    showNotify("Player left! Now: " .. count .. " players")
end)
    end
})

AddButton(Tab1o, {
    Name = "Sá»‘ ngÃ y chÆ¡i roblox",
    Callback = function()
      -- TÃ­nh sá»‘ ngÃ y tham gia Roblox (Simple Version)
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local player = Players.LocalPlayer

local function showNotify(text)
    game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
        Title = "Account Info",
        Text = text,
        Duration = 8
    })
end

-- Kiá»ƒm tra AccountAge (náº¿u cÃ³)
player:WaitForChild("PlayerGui")

-- Thá»­ láº¥y AccountAge
local accountAgeDays = player.AccountAge
if accountAgeDays then
    showNotify("Account age: " .. accountAgeDays .. " days")
else
    -- PhÆ°Æ¡ng phÃ¡p dá»± phÃ²ng: dÃ¹ng JoinDate
    local joinDate = player:GetJoinDate()
    if joinDate then
        local currentDate = DateTime.now()
        local difference = currentDate.UnixTimestamp - joinDate.UnixTimestamp
        local days = math.floor(difference / (60 * 60 * 24))
        showNotify("Joined: " .. days .. " days ago")
    else
        showNotify("Cannot get account info")
    end
end
    end
})

AddButton(Tab1o, {
    Name = "sá»‘ thá»i gian trong server",
    Callback = function()
      -- TÃ­nh thá»i gian trong server
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local player = Players.LocalPlayer

local joinTime = tick()

local function updateNotify()
    local currentTime = tick()
    local seconds = math.floor(currentTime - joinTime)
    local minutes = math.floor(seconds / 60)
    local hours = math.floor(minutes / 60)
    
    seconds = seconds % 60
    minutes = minutes % 60
    
    local timeText = ""
    if hours > 0 then
        timeText = hours .. "h " .. minutes .. "m " .. seconds .. "s"
    elseif minutes > 0 then
        timeText = minutes .. "m " .. seconds .. "s"
    else
        timeText = seconds .. "s"
    end
    
    game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
        Title = "Time in Server",
        Text = timeText,
        Duration = 1
    })
end

-- Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ khi vÃ o server
game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
    Title = "Server Time",
    Text = "Started timer",
    Duration = 3
})

-- Cáº­p nháº­t má»—i 30 giÃ¢y
while true do
    wait(30)
    updateNotify()
end
    end
})

AddButton(Tabo, {
