      -- HeadOnlyUniversal.lua
-- LocalScript: Hoáº¡t Ä‘á»™ng cho cáº£ R6 vÃ  R15 - Client Hack
-- DÃ¹ng executor inject

local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local RunService = game:GetService("RunService")
local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")

local player = Players.LocalPlayer
local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()
local humanoid = character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
local rootPart = character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
local head = character:WaitForChild("Head")

-- XÃ¡c Ä‘á»‹nh R6 hay R15
local isR15 = humanoid.RigType == Enum.HumanoidRigType.R15
local active = false
local originalStates = {}

-- Biáº¿n Ä‘iá»u khiá»ƒn láº¯c
local bobSpeed = 3
local bobHeight = 0.5
local bobConnection
local floating = false

-- HÃ m áº©n toÃ n bá»™ body trá»« Ä‘áº§u (cho cáº£ R6 vÃ  R15)
local function hideAllExceptHead()
    if not character then return end
    
    originalStates = {}
    
    -- Xá»­ lÃ½ cho R6
    if not isR15 then
        local r6Parts = {"Torso", "Left Arm", "Right Arm", "Left Leg", "Right Leg"}
        
        for _, partName in pairs(r6Parts) do
            local part = character:FindFirstChild(partName)
            if part then
                originalStates[part] = {
                    Transparency = part.Transparency,
                    LocalTransparencyModifier = part.LocalTransparencyModifier or 0
                }
                part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1
                part.CanCollide = false
            end
        end
        
        -- Xá»­ lÃ½ cÃ¡c parts khÃ¡c
        for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") and not table.find(r6Parts, part.Name) and part.Name ~= "Head" then
                originalStates[part] = {
                    Transparency = part.Transparency,
                    LocalTransparencyModifier = part.LocalTransparencyModifier or 0
                }
                part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1
                part.CanCollide = false
            end
        end
        
    -- Xá»­ lÃ½ cho R15
    else
        -- R15 cÃ³ nhiá»u parts hÆ¡n
        local r15Parts = {
            "UpperTorso", "LowerTorso",
            "LeftUpperArm", "LeftLowerArm", "LeftHand",
            "RightUpperArm", "RightLowerArm", "RightHand",
            "LeftUpperLeg", "LeftLowerLeg", "LeftFoot",
            "RightUpperLeg", "RightLowerLeg", "RightFoot"
        }
        
        for _, partName in pairs(r15Parts) do
            local part = character:FindFirstChild(partName)
            if part then
                originalStates[part] = {
                    Transparency = part.Transparency,
                    LocalTransparencyModifier = part.LocalTransparencyModifier or 0
                }
                part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1
                part.CanCollide = false
            end
        end
        
        -- áº¨n táº¥t cáº£ MeshParts khÃ¡c
        for _, part in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
            if (part:IsA("BasePart") or part:IsA("MeshPart")) and part.Name ~= "Head" then
                if not originalStates[part] then
                    originalStates[part] = {
                        Transparency = part.Transparency,
                        LocalTransparencyModifier = part.LocalTransparencyModifier or 0
                    }
                    part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1
                    part.CanCollide = false
                end
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- áº¨n accessories cho cáº£ 2
    for _, accessory in pairs(character:GetChildren()) do
        if accessory:IsA("Accessory") then
            local handle = accessory:FindFirstChild("Handle")
            if handle then
                originalStates[handle] = {
                    Transparency = handle.Transparency,
                    LocalTransparencyModifier = handle.LocalTransparencyModifier or 0
                }
                handle.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1
                handle.CanCollide = false
            end
        end
    end

    local tool = character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Tool")
    if tool then
        for _, part in pairs(tool:GetDescendants()) do
            if part:IsA("BasePart") then
                originalStates[part] = {
                    Transparency = part.Transparency,
                    LocalTransparencyModifier = part.LocalTransparencyModifier or 0
                }
                part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1
                part.CanCollide = false
            end
        end
    end
    
    print("[HACK] ÄÃ£ áº©n body (" .. (isR15 and "R15" or "R6") .. ")")
end

-- HÃ m táº¡o Ã¡nh sÃ¡ng Ä‘á»
local function createRedAura()
    if not head then return nil end
    
    -- XÃ³a cÅ©
    for _, child in pairs(head:GetChildren()) do
        if child:IsA("PointLight") or child:IsA("SurfaceLight") or child:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
            child:Destroy()
        end
    end
    
    local effects = {}
    
    -- Point Light Ä‘á»
    local pointLight = Instance.new("PointLight")
    pointLight.Name = "GhostLightRed"
    pointLight.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
    pointLight.Range = 25
    pointLight.Brightness = 3
    pointLight.Shadows = true
    pointLight.Parent = head
    table.insert(effects, pointLight)
    
    -- Particle Ä‘á»
    local particles = Instance.new("ParticleEmitter")
    particles.Name = "RedSmoke"
    particles.Texture = "rbxassetid://242295229"
    particles.Color = ColorSequence.new(Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0))
    particles.Transparency = NumberSequence.new(0.7)
    particles.Size = NumberSequence.new(1.5)
    particles.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(1.5)
    particles.Rate = 40
    particles.Speed = NumberRange.new(3)
    particles.VelocitySpread = 180
    particles.Parent = head
    table.insert(effects, particles)
    
    -- Glow effect
    local glow = Instance.new("SurfaceLight")
    glow.Name = "HeadGlow"
    glow.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 50, 50)
    glow.Range = 20
    glow.Brightness = 2
    glow.Face = Enum.NormalId.Front
    glow.Parent = head
    table.insert(effects, glow)
    
    return effects
end

-- HÃ m láº¯c Ä‘áº§u cho R6
local function headBobR6()
    if not head or not character.Torso then return end
    
    local startTime = tick()
    
    bobConnection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        if not head or not active then
            if bobConnection then bobConnection:Disconnect() end
            return
        end
        
        local time = tick() - startTime
        
        -- TÃ­nh láº¯c
        local bobX = math.sin(time * bobSpeed * 1.2) * 0.3
        local bobY = math.sin(time * bobSpeed) * bobHeight + 1.5
        local bobZ = math.cos(time * bobSpeed * 0.8) * 0.2
        
        -- TÃ¬m Neck joint
        local neck = head:FindFirstChild("Neck")
        if neck then
            -- Láº¯c báº±ng joint
            local rotation = CFrame.Angles(
                math.sin(time * bobSpeed * 0.6) * 0.15,
                math.sin(time * bobSpeed * 0.9) * 0.25,
                math.sin(time * bobSpeed * 0.3) * 0.1
            )
            neck.C1 = CFrame.new(bobX, bobY, bobZ) * rotation
        else
            -- Fallback: di chuyá»ƒn trá»±c tiáº¿p head
            head.CFrame = CFrame.new(head.Position) * CFrame.Angles(
                math.sin(time * 0.5) * 0.2,
                time * 1.5,
                math.sin(time * 0.3) * 0.1
            )
        end
    end)
end

-- HÃ m láº¯c Ä‘áº§u cho R15
local function headBobR15()
    if not head then return end
    
    local startTime = tick()
    
    bobConnection = RunService.RenderStepped:Connect(function(dt)
        if not head or not active then
            if bobConnection then bobConnection:Disconnect() end
            return
        end
        
        local time = tick() - startTime
        
        -- R15 cÃ³ NeckRigAttachment
        local neckRig = head:FindFirstChild("NeckRigAttachment")
        if neckRig then
            -- Di chuyá»ƒn attachment point
            local bobOffset = Vector3.new(
                math.sin(time * bobSpeed * 1.3) * 0.25,
                math.sin(time * bobSpeed) * bobHeight * 0.8 + 0.2,
                math.cos(time * bobSpeed * 1.1) * 0.2
            )
            
            -- Xoay Ä‘áº§u
            head.CFrame = head.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(
                math.sin(time * bobSpeed * 0.7) * 0.1,
                math.sin(time * bobSpeed * 1.2) * 0.3,
                math.sin(time * bobSpeed * 0.4) * 0.05
            )
        end
        
        -- Float effect
        if floating then
            local floatY = math.sin(time * 2) * 0.2
            head.Position = head.Position + Vector3.new(0, floatY * dt * 10, 0)
        end
    end)
end

-- HÃ m báº­t float mode
local function toggleFloat()
    floating = not floating
    print("[HACK] Float mode: " .. (floating and "ON" or "OFF"))
end

-- KhÃ´i phá»¥c toÃ n bá»™
local function restoreAll()
    active = false
    
    if bobConnection then
        bobConnection:Disconnect()
        bobConnection = nil
    end
    
    -- KhÃ´i phá»¥c parts
    for part, state in pairs(originalStates) do
        if part and part.Parent then
            part.LocalTransparencyModifier = state.LocalTransparencyModifier or 0
            part.CanCollide = true
            part.Transparency = state.Transparency or 0
        end
    end
    
    -- Reset head position
    if head then
        -- Reset neck joint
        local neck = head:FindFirstChild("Neck")
        if neck then
            neck.C1 = CFrame.new(0, 1.5, 0)
        end
        
        -- XÃ³a effects
        for _, child in pairs(head:GetChildren()) do
            if child:IsA("PointLight") or child:IsA("SurfaceLight") or 
               child:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or child.Name == "GhostSound" then
                child:Destroy()
            end
        end
    end
    
    print("[HACK] ÄÃ£ khÃ´i phá»¥c toÃ n bá»™")
end

-- Toggle chÃ­nh
local function toggleHeadOnly()
    active = not active
    
    if active then
        print("[")
        
        -- áº¨n body
        hideAllExceptHead()
        
        -- Táº¡o aura
        createRedAura()
        
        -- Báº­t láº¯c Ä‘áº§u
        if isR15 then
            headBobR15()
        else
            headBobR6()
        end
        
        -- Ã‚m thanh
        playGhostSound()
        
    else
        print("[HACK] Táº¯t HEAD-ONLY mode")
        restoreAll()
    end
end

-- Ã‚m thanh ma
local ghostSound
local function playGhostSound()
    if not head then return end
    
    if ghostSound then
        ghostSound:Stop()
        ghostSound:Destroy()
    end
    
    ghostSound = Instance.new("Sound")
    ghostSound.Name = "GhostSound"
    ghostSound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://138081500"
    ghostSound.Looped = true
    ghostSound.Volume = 0.4
    ghostSound.Parent = head
    ghostSound:Play()
end

            bobSpeed = math.max(bobSpeed - 0.3, 0.5)
            print("[HACK] Tá»‘c Ä‘á»™: " .. bobSpeed)
        end
    end
end)

-- Server Hopper Ä‘Æ¡n giáº£n
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")

local placeId = game.PlaceId
local currentJobId = game.JobId

-- ThÃ´ng bÃ¡o
local function notify(text)
    game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
        Title = "Hopper",
        Text = text,
        Duration = 3
    })
end

-- Láº¥y servers
local function getServers()
    local url = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. placeId .. "/servers/Public?limit=50"
    
    local success, result = pcall(function()
        return HttpService:GetAsync(url, true)
    end)
    
    if success then
        local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(result)
        return data.data
    end
    return {}
end

-- Hop server
local function hop()
    notify("Finding server...")
    
    local servers = getServers()
    
    for _, server in pairs(servers) do
        if server.id ~= currentJobId and server.playing < 10 then
            notify("Joining new server...")
            TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, server.id)
            return
        end
    end
    
    notify("No good servers found")
end

AddButton(Tab2o, {
    Name = "hop server",
    Callback = function()
      hop();
    end
})

    Name = "hop server Ã­t ngÆ°á»i",
    Callback = function()
      -- Server Hopper tÃ¬m server Ã­t ngÆ°á»i
local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")

local placeId = game.PlaceId
local currentJobId = game.JobId

-- ThÃ´ng bÃ¡o
game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
    Title = "Server Hopper",
    Text = "Äang tÃ¬m server Ã­t ngÆ°á»i...",
    Duration = 3
})

-- Láº¥y danh sÃ¡ch server
local url = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. placeId .. "/servers/Public?limit=100"

local success, response = pcall(function()
    return HttpService:GetAsync(url, true)
end)

if success then
    local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(response)
    local servers = data.data
    
    -- TÃ¬m server Ã­t ngÆ°á»i nháº¥t
    local bestServer = nil
    local lowestPlayers = math.huge
    
    for _, server in pairs(servers) do
        -- Bá» qua server hiá»‡n táº¡i
        if server.id ~= currentJobId then
            local playerCount = server.playing or 0
            
            -- TÃ¬m server cÃ³ Ã­t ngÆ°á»i nháº¥t
            if playerCount < lowestPlayers and playerCount > 0 then
                lowestPlayers = playerCount
                bestServer = server
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- Hop náº¿u tÃ¬m Ä‘Æ°á»£c server
    if bestServer then
        game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
            Title = "Found Server",
            Text = "Server cÃ³ " .. lowestPlayers .. " ngÆ°á»i",
            Duration = 3
        })
        
        wait(1)
        
        TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, bestServer.id)
    else
        game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
            Title = "Lá»—i",
            Text = "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y server nÃ o",
            Duration = 3
        })
    end
else
    game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
        Title = "Lá»—i",
        Text = "KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ láº¥y danh sÃ¡ch server",
        Duration = 3
    })
end
    end
})

AddButton(Tab2o, {
    Name = "Join server trá»‘ng",
    Callback = function()
      -- TÃ¬m server trá»‘ng (khÃ´ng cÃ³ ai)
local TeleportService = game:GetService("TeleportService")
local HttpService = game:GetService("HttpService")

local placeId = game.PlaceId
local currentJobId = game.JobId

-- ThÃ´ng bÃ¡o
game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
    Title = "Finding Server",
    Text = "Äang tÃ¬m server trá»‘ng...",
    Duration = 3
})

-- Láº¥y danh sÃ¡ch server
local url = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. placeId .. "/servers/Public?limit=100"

local success, response = pcall(function()
    return HttpService:GetAsync(url, true)
end)

if success then
    local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(response)
    local servers = data.data
    
    -- TÃ¬m server khÃ´ng cÃ³ ai
    local emptyServer = nil
    
    for _, server in pairs(servers) do
        -- Bá» qua server hiá»‡n táº¡i
        if server.id ~= currentJobId then
            local playerCount = server.playing or 0
            
            -- Náº¿u server khÃ´ng cÃ³ ai
            if playerCount == 0 then
                emptyServer = server
                break
            end
        end
    end
    
    -- Hop náº¿u tÃ¬m Ä‘Æ°á»£c server trá»‘ng
    if emptyServer then
        game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
            Title = "Found Empty Server",
            Text = "ÄÃ£ tÃ¬m tháº¥y server trá»‘ng!",
            Duration = 3
        })
        
        wait(1)
        
        TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, emptyServer.id)
    else
        -- Náº¿u khÃ´ng cÃ³ server trá»‘ng, tÃ¬m server Ã­t ngÆ°á»i nháº¥t
        local bestServer = nil
        local lowestPlayers = math.huge
        
        for _, server in pairs(servers) do
            if server.id ~= currentJobId then
                local playerCount = server.playing or 0
                
                if playerCount < lowestPlayers and playerCount >= 1 then
                    lowestPlayers = playerCount
                    bestServer = server
                end
            end
        end
        
        if bestServer then
            game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
                Title = "No Empty Servers",
                Text = "Server Ã­t nháº¥t: " .. lowestPlayers .. " ngÆ°á»i",
                Duration = 3
            })
            
            wait(1)
            
            TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(placeId, bestServer.id)
        else
            game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
                Title = "Lá»—i",
                Text = "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y server nÃ o",
                Duration = 3
            })
        end
    end
else
    game.StarterGui:SetCore("SendNotification", {
        Title = "Lá»—i",
        Text = "KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ káº¿t ná»‘i",
        Duration = 3
    })
end
    end
})
